Fourth Plenary Session Holds Fourth General Assembly Yesterday

Re-examining the Proposal to Improve the Central Party Headquarters Organization

Banning Opium within One Year with the Strictest Methods

(Nanjing) The Fourth National Congress of the Chinese Nationalist Party held its fourth meeting at the Fourth Plenary Session meeting place at 8:00 AM on the 18th. 347 representatives attended, 13 non-voting delegates, 32 central committee members, and 4 non-voting alternate central committee members. Yu Youren presided, with Ye Chucang as secretary-general. Wang Zizhuang, Zhu Yunguang, Xu Jingzhi, Hong Lanyou, Luo Shishi, and Pu Liangdu recorded the proceedings. The agenda and the main points of the resolutions of the conference are recorded separately below.

(A) Reports: (1) Reading the minutes of the third meeting; (2) Secretariat report on documents (including 9 congratulatory telegrams, 12 petition documents, and 4 representative documents); (3) Presidium report on the list of replacement representatives; (4) Zhejiang Provincial Party Affairs Report; (5) Yunnan Provincial Party Affairs Report; (6) Report on the party affairs of the branch directly under the Khmer Republic; (7) Report on the party affairs of the branch directly under Tahiti.

(B) Summary of Resolutions: (1) The proposal of the Central Executive Committee to improve the organization of the Central Party Headquarters, the proposal of the Hebei Provincial Party Department to improve the organization of the Party, and the proposal of Comrade Huang Bingheng and 26 others to organize a special air force party headquarters were handed over to the Party Affairs Group of the Proposal Review Committee for re-examination. (2) The proposal of Comrade He Ruqun and 23 others to earnestly protect overseas Chinese was approved in accordance with the review report of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Group of the Proposal Review Committee. (3) The proposal of Comrade He Ruqun and 28 others to reorganize overseas Chinese education was approved in accordance with the review report of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Group of the Proposal Review Committee. (4) The proposal of Comrade Wu Zhaohai and 22 others to continue to provide relief to unemployed overseas Chinese in order to take care of the national dignity and maintain the people's livelihood, and the proposal of Comrade Shen Hongbai and 21 others that the government should find ways to provide relief to unemployed overseas Chinese returning to China according to the regulations were discussed together and decided to be approved in accordance with the review report of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Group of the Proposal Review Committee. (5) The proposal of Comrade He Jinquan and 23 others that overseas Chinese who are deported back to China for official reasons should be given appropriate placement was approved in accordance with the review report of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Group of the Proposal Review Committee. (6) The proposal of Comrade He Jian and 27 others to dredge the rivers and lakes as soon as possible to develop water conservancy was handed over to the Construction and Industry Groups of the Proposal Review Committee for re-examination. (7) In accordance with the last words of the Premier, opium should be banned. The task of devising the most rigorous and appropriate methods to ban opium within one year will be assigned to the relevant authorities of the National Government. (Special dispatch, 18th)

Meeting to Relieve the Coal Shortage Continued Yesterday

(Nanjing) The meeting to relieve the Yangtze River coal industry continued its second session on the 18th. Representatives from the Ministry of Finance and the shipping association, including Yu Hede, attended. The following issues were discussed: 1. If there is excessive coal inventory due to high costs, a request can be made to estimate and borrow against the coal price to facilitate turnover; 2. Develop new mines to increase production; 3. Request the establishment of low coal and coke transportation rates; 4. Reduce taxes; 5. Reward and protect the coal mining industry; 6. Extend long routes to build seaports; 7. Quickly repair damaged vehicles on various routes. Corresponding decisions were made on all issues. (18th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways telegraphed the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, the Coal Industry Association, and the China National Coal Production and Sales Federation, reiterating the measures stipulated in the case of temporarily suspending coal transportation price increases on the Jiaoji Railway for three months: 1. Coal exported from Shandong Province should be transported to Shanghai as much as possible, solely for domestic use; 2. During the national crisis, coal prices must not increase; 3. Coal should continue to be supplied to the Jiaoji Railway at low prices. These measures have been agreed upon and promised by the representatives of the chamber, and should not be changed. If mines with existing contracts and government-approved foreign investment are excluded, then most of the coal mines along the Jiaoji Railway are jointly operated with Japanese investment, and the coal produced is also shipped to Japan. Only a small amount is usually sold to Shanghai. Now that price increases are prohibited, it will inevitably still be transported to Japan to achieve the purpose of making profits. Coal merchants are using the domestic coal shortage as an excuse to call for reduced transportation costs, but the result is only to supply cheap coal to Japanese users, while coal merchants profit from it. The domestic coal shortage still cannot be relieved. The association should find ways to correct this situation to achieve thorough relief, and we hope for a detailed reply. (18th Special Dispatch)

Ministry of Railways Formulates National Highway Construction Plan

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways has formulated a national highway construction plan. The first phase will prioritize the construction of the entire Beijing-Guilin line, as well as parts of the Beijing-Yunnan-Kangding line, the Beijing-Tibet line, the Fujian-Xinjiang line, and the Suiyuan-Xinjiang line, approximately 16,000 li in length, to be completed within six years. The funding plan will use the revenue from the national gasoline tax, vehicle license tax, and driver's license fees. After deducting the amount allocated to the public debt fund, the remainder will be used exclusively for road construction. The plan has been submitted to the Executive Yuan and referred to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation and inclusion in the national budget to facilitate implementation. According to statistics, the total length of highways in all provinces of the country was only 2,000 li in 1926, but by the end of 1930, it had reached over 51,000 li. (18th Special Dispatch)

International Important Telegrams

Developments in German Politics

National Socialism Thriving

Possibility of Liaison with the Central Party

Berlin dispatch, 17th (National News) The current internal political situation in Germany shows rapid development, which is closely related to the general trend in Europe. In the Hesse election a few days ago, the National Socialist Party won a great victory. The results of this move greatly affect the Catholic Central Party, because the party's position is really in a dilemma. In the future, will it unite with the left-wing parties to form a new government that is precarious, or will it combine with the National Socialist Party? If it does combine with the National Socialist Party, the whole country will follow suit, and the various states will follow suit. Here, political leaders do not deny the possibility of the Central Party and the National Socialist Party discussing the link, and although they do not actively promote the combination, they think that the matter is not completely impossible. Premier Bruning's personal views may also be the same. He does not agree with National Socialism, but he feels that since National Socialism is now so magnificent, in terms of principle, it should be given a chance to gradually change its negative attitude and adopt a proactive policy. Furthermore, Bruning also wants to use the National Socialist Party to control a part of the political power, thereby destroying the united front of the right wing. The Nationalist Party and the Nationalist Party, which were previously combined with the National Socialist Party, are excluded from Bruning's new plan. Bruning is secretly colluding with the National Socialist Party on the one hand, but on the other hand, he has not abandoned his long-standing contact with the Socialist Party. The Socialist Party has now demanded that Bruning publicly and clearly reject the National Socialist Party and cancel all its ruling movements, and declared that if Bruning cannot do this, it will be difficult to continue to cooperate in the future, and will join the non-governmental faction to support the reorganization of the Congress, which is tantamount to the death knell of the Bruning government, and Bruning can not call on any ability without the support of the Socialist Party.

French Chamber of Deputies Discusses Foreign Policy

Paris dispatch, 18th (Havas) The agenda of the Chamber of Deputies is the discussion of foreign policy questions. Briand attended and answered, and did not leave the House until 6 pm. The leader of the left-wing Radical Party spoke about relations with Russia, saying that France's failure to trade with the Soviet Union has led to closer relations with other countries, which he deeply regretted. He also said that when France and Soviet Russia conducted treaty negotiations in 1927, newspapers, under the influence of a certain British and American oil trust, opposed the treaty and made it impossible to establish.

Page 11

Receiving International Important Telegrams

Now, if we want to reopen negotiations, the Soviet Union's dumping policy will be a stumbling block, and the intervention of industrialists will also have an impact. For the present plan, we should first set a non-aggression treaty and an immigration treaty for overseas Chinese as the first step in the process, and then engage in negotiations to conclude a formal commercial treaty, as well as to conclude an agreement to resolve debts and to determine the purchase of goods and the extension of payments, because the Soviet Union recognizes its debts to France, but requires France to borrow from it. Then a member of the Social Radical Party stood up and gave a speech, talking about the financial relations between France and Germany and the policy of the United States toward Europe. He Yun, Europe can not rely on the United States, and the United States can not ask for Europe. We have 400 million US dollars in cash, but we are debtors to the United States. The fall of the US dollar is beneficial to us. Although the Americans know that they cannot be isolated, they do not want to join the League of Nations. Finally, the member of parliament said that international compromise is necessary.

The U.S. State Department Can Do Nothing

Washington, according to reports received by the U.S. State Department, the Japanese are buying a large amount of refined Nitro for gunpowder manufacturing in the U.S. market, which is very noteworthy at this time. The U.S. State Department claims that prohibiting the export of such commodities is beyond the authority of the President and must be executed by an act of Congress. Gandhi Demands Jurisdiction over the Army

London dispatch, 18th (Reuters) Gandhi said today at the meeting of the Structures Committee of the Indian Round Table Conference, "If you British officials and people are really well-intentioned towards India, the Indian Army should be entirely under our jurisdiction. I think this is a necessary condition for the British to be well-intentioned. I have not asked for the withdrawal of the British army." Gandhi's strong attitude made the British representatives Reading and Sankey feel very difficult. Some Indian representatives did not agree with Gandhi's extreme demands.

Calcutta dispatch, 18th (Reuters) The Indian Swaraj Party is gradually becoming uneasy about the progress of the Indian Round Table Conference in London and Gandhi's delayed return to India. Nehru said in a speech today that without a new struggle, it is impossible to achieve the goal of autonomy. He advocated starting a pan-Indian passive resistance as soon as possible, without waiting for Gandhi to return to India.

Britain and France Increase Tariff Barriers

London dispatch, 18th (Reuters) The financial bill of Minister of Commerce Runciman, which allows the Department of Commerce to increase tariffs on goods imported into the United Kingdom in large quantities, up to 100% of the value of the goods, has been passed in the House of Commons. Runciman said that the average monthly import of foreign goods is 20.6 million pounds, which is now increased to 35 million pounds. Except for food, beverages, tobacco, raw materials and unfinished goods, all others must be taxed uniformly, up to double the price of the goods, to prevent dumping. According to the new bill, goods imported from overseas autonomous regions can get a 100% preferential tax compared with foreign goods, which is a major concession by the government to the Imperial Free Trade Party.

Paris dispatch, 18th (Reuters) The French government today submitted an important bill to increase import taxes. The tax on semi-finished products will be increased from 2% to 4%, and the tax on finished products will be increased from 2% to 6%. The import tax on raw materials will remain at 2% and will not be increased.

Important News

Resurgence of the Tao'ang War

Detailed Account of the Fierce Battles on the 12th and 13th

Honzō Shigeru's Ultimatum and Our Reply

Harbin Dispatch: The Japanese army's attempt to attack Hei was unsuccessful, suffering a defeat between Tailai and the Jiangqiao bridge. Feeling quite humiliated, they have been working hard to replenish their troops in an attempt to break through our line of defense in one fell swoop. At 12:00 noon on the 12th, they first used intimidation tactics to issue an ultimatum to Ma Zhanshan, Chairman of Hei Province, demanding a reply by 12:00 midnight. The original ultimatum contained three restrictions, roughly translated as follows: "This officer requests the following from your side: (1) Chairman Ma Zhanshan should step down; (2) The Heilongjiang Province army should withdraw from Qiqihar; (3) A portion of the Japanese army, for the sake of ensuring the safety of the Tao'ang line, should begin its advance from the Ang'angxi station on the Tao'ang line. Please submit a reply to this by 12:00 midnight on November 12th. Respectfully addressed to Chairman Ma Zhanshan of Heilongjiang, Commander of the Kwantung Army, Honzō Shigeru, November 12th, Showa Year 6," and so on. This document was delivered to the Hei Province government by Hayashi, a naval attache from the Japanese consulate in Hei City. After receiving it, Ma Zhanshan immediately sent an urgent telegram to Beiping, requesting instructions from Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang. He received a reply from Zhang, stating: "(1) Is this ultimatum issued by Honzō personally, or does it represent the Tokyo government? (2) Honzō's representative, Hayashi, did not carry any identification, and a mere telegram is insufficient proof. (3) The ultimatum arrived at noon, but before waiting for a reply, Japanese cavalry and artillery units launched a fierce attack on our positions. What is the reason for this? Even if we take a step back and assume Hayashi represents Honzō, and Honzō represents the Japanese government, there is no reason to demand that our army retreat. We should firmly reject it and defend to the end," and so on. The war began at 2:15 PM on the 12th. Ma Zhanshan left the ultimatum unanswered until noon on the 13th, when he replied, rejecting the three demands, stating: "(1) Stepping down is not impossible, but it requires an order from the Chinese government and the dispatch of personnel to take over. Even if the government appoints Zhang Haipeng, the political power will not be handed over. (2) Regarding the withdrawal of troops, we have the right to do so within our own Chinese territory, and the Japanese side has no right to interfere. (3) Ang'angxi Station is a station jointly operated by China and Russia. Your request for withdrawal contradicts Representative Yoshizawa's statement in the League of Nations that "Japan has no territorial ambitions." Furthermore, I am ordered to defend the territory, and I cannot comply until I receive a clear order from my government to abandon it. At the same time, in terms of legal facts, it is not something your country should demand," and so on. Regarding this reply and the original text of Honzō's ultimatum, Ma has telegraphed our representative to the League of Nations, Shi Zhaoji, instructing him to present it to the assembly. As for the war, before 2:15 PM on the 12th, the Japanese army first used more than 500 cavalry and artillery soldiers to launch a fierce attack on the left flank of our cavalry brigade under Wu, stationed in Wunotou Zhangjiahuayuan (in the three rooms of the Daxing station), firing like a string of pearls. Our cavalry was suppressed and chased, and the position was on the verge of wavering. Fortunately, the soldiers were determined and persevered in resisting. The Japanese army attacked fiercely for 40 minutes but failed to achieve its goal and retreated. Our army also suffered casualties at that time, including two deputy company commanders, one adjutant, and fourteen soldiers killed in battle. The war briefly subsided, but before an hour had passed, the Japanese army launched another attack with a large force, using all its strength to deal with our army, encircling our line of defense, and using eight heavy artillery pieces to fiercely attack our cavalry and artillery positions. The Japanese army, with more than 6,000 soldiers, was divided into three branches, with brigade commanders Hase and Amano each responsible for the left and right wings, and Mori, commander of the Manchurian Railway garrison, acting as the central commander. More than ten aircraft also dropped bombs from the air. Their heavy artillery was extremely powerful, and many sections of our trenches were destroyed. Yuan Zonggu, the commander-in-chief at the front, seeing that Wu's brigade was in danger, transferred a regiment from Zhang Dianjiu's brigade from the second and third lines of defense to join the front and help resist the enemy. After 6:00 PM, the enemy army, unable to gain an advantage, retreated in large numbers and switched to artillery attacks, firing hundreds of rounds. Our army also returned fire with artillery. At 7:30 PM, the artillery attack stopped, and the Japanese army resumed using small teams of cavalry, about a dozen men per group, to repeatedly harass our positions. Our army retaliated, and they fled far away. If we did not attack, they would approach our trenches. The fighting completely stopped after 8:00 PM. After 11:00 PM in the evening, they began to attack again. Until about 1:00 AM on the 13th, they twice charged our trenches with handheld machine guns, but were repelled by our army. At about 2:00 AM, the war resumed. At about 5:00 AM on the morning of the 13th, the Japanese army attacked our Xinlitu village position again with more than 500 soldiers. At about 7:00 AM, two aircraft provided cover in the air, dropping more than 30 bombs. Armored vehicles also fired artillery from across the river. At about 10:00 AM, they retreated again without achieving anything. At noon, another aircraft came to reconnoiter our line of defense in the Jiangqiao area, dropping six bombs, killing five of our soldiers and wounding two. They were repelled by our army's artillery fire. During the two days, the Japanese army attacked continuously, and the officers and soldiers at the front were unable to rest day and night. Ma Zhanshan, fearing that the soldiers were too tired and that the line of defense would be difficult to consolidate, urgently telegraphed the independent cavalry eighth brigade under Cheng Zhiyuan, stationed in Manzhouli Zhalannuoer, and the Gan and Liu regiments to go to the front to take over the defense. The Tu regiment arrived in Ang'angxi on the evening of the 13th, and the Liu regiment will arrive tomorrow. Zhang Haipeng's troops did not participate in this war. It is said that because his soldiers were unwilling to be oppressed by the Japanese army, they lacked fighting spirit and did not listen to Japanese orders. A part of Zhang's army, which had detoured to Jingxing, has been contacted and reorganized by Ma Zhanshan, and there has been considerable progress. Another piece of news is that Zhang Haipeng himself, feeling that the Japanese army was coercing him too much, killed the Japanese who was monitoring him on the evening of the 12th and fled with more than ten of his confidants. Zhang's troops lost their commander, leading to disintegration. Whether this is true or not remains to be investigated. (14th)

The Great American Evening Post's Harbin dispatch on the 16th stated: According to a long-distance telephone call from Qiqihar, yesterday the Japanese army ambushed the side of the Chinese army on the Tao'ang Road, attempting to cut off the transportation line. The fierce battle lasted all day and was almost a complete annihilation. General Ma Zhanshan's troops captured 500 Japanese soldiers, and also captured two Japanese field guns and countless bullets. The Japanese casualties totaled more than 60. The Japanese army used a right-wing encirclement tactic, aiming to cut off the transportation line between the Chinese army on the front line and the headquarters in Ang'angxi. General Ma Zhanshan used 4,000 cavalry to fight back, finally surrounding the Japanese army and isolating it from the armored vehicles that followed to provide cover. Although the Japanese army used aircraft to drop bombs, the damage was minimal because of the sandy soil. From 8:00 AM in the morning, the fierce battle lasted until dusk, almost completely annihilating the Japanese army. The last remaining part of the Japanese army took advantage of the dusk, with the cover of the armored vehicle's artillery fire, to break out of the encirclement and retreat to the Nenjiang River bank. The Chinese army's line of defense then advanced several miles, about 30 miles from Ang'angxi Station and about six miles from the Nenjiang Bridge. The people of Harbin were very excited when they heard the news of the great victory of Ma Zhanshan's army, as if they had been electrified. Various groups and schools raised funds and winter clothes and transported them to the front lines to comfort the soldiers. It is said that hundreds of students have gone to join Ma's army. The Harbin military police now have 10,000 road protection soldiers under Ding Chao and 5,600 policemen under Wang Renhua (transliteration), both of whom expressed sympathy for Ma Zhanshan. Recently, Zhang Jinghui's newly formed security team of 2,500 people heard today that about 4,000 soldiers from Jilin province who were unwilling to be commanded by Xi Qia gathered at the Ashihe Station on the Middle East Road, all of whom were trained soldiers. It is said that a part of them have gone to Qiqihar to join the war of resistance against Japan. The Harbin Times, run by the Japanese in this area, printed the news of Puyi's restoration in Shenyang on the front page in large characters today, saying that Puyi had been restored yesterday, but the enthronement ceremony still needs to be postponed. It also said that the Japanese have reached an agreement with Puyi to resolve all outstanding issues in the three northeastern provinces. It also carried a speech by Uchida, the president of the South Manchuria Railway, saying that the Japanese army not only cannot withdraw, but must increase greatly to maintain the Japanese position.

The Harbin dispatch of the 17th of the North China Daily News stated that several Japanese aircraft dropped bombs on Fularji town on the Middle East Railway to the west of Qiqihar, destroying railway houses and warehouses, fearing that they would attack Qiqihar.

The Inside Story of the Japanese Smuggling Puyi out of Tianjin

Beiping Dispatch: After Doihara, who called himself a "China expert," arrived in Tianjin with Jin Liang on the 2nd of this month, he went to visit Puyi to persuade him to go through the pass to restore the throne. Puyi dared not agree, and Doihara threatened him with dangerous words and left in disappointment. On the night of the 6th, a bomb was found in a fruit basket in Puyi's residence, which was also a coercive trick by Doihara. At the same time, Doihara and others sought other ways and went to Zheng Xiaoxu, a remnant of the Qing dynasty, with Jin Liang, to explain the plan of restoration in detail, saying that if Puyi was restored to the throne, Japan would definitely provide assistance with strength. Zheng's mind was simple, only knowing loyalty to the emperor but not patriotism. Moreover, his son, Yan Zuo, was blinded by greed for profit, and he incited his father, saying that the Republic of China had really let down the royal family (probably referring to being driven out of the palace and stopping the preferential treatment fee). Now that there is this opportunity, the Japanese can be used to avenge this shame. Even if it fails, at the very least, he can move to Tokyo like the Yi Wang of Korea and enjoy happiness, and so on. Zheng was moved by this and agreed. He then went to visit Puyi with Doihara and Jin Liang, making various inducements. Puyi was originally a child, how could he know the general trend? However, because many former Qing officials still opposed it, and the Japanese side wanted Puyi to establish a new country title, he was even more dissatisfied and showed hesitation. Therefore, Zheng and Jin negotiated with Doihara again. Finally, Doihara said that if Mr. Puyi is willing to restore the throne, then regarding the issue of the country title, whether to establish a new name or restore the old name, it is all possible. It is also no problem to continue using the Xuantong era name. At present, please Mr. Pu first go to Dalian, and everything can be discussed at length, and so on. Jin Liang and Zheng Xiaoxu used this to flatter Puyi again. This confused and mediocre child was forced by internal and external forces, so he disregarded everything and decided to relive his old dream of being an emperor. Doihara's plan of instigation has already succeeded, and he also fears that the Chinese side will pay attention to this matter. In order to divert attention, he betrayed Zhang Bi, Li Jichun, etc., and recruited plainclothes teams, which led to the Tianjin Incident on the 8th. Puyi took advantage of the plainclothes teams' disturbances on the night of the 10th, took his father Zai Cheng and his wife, as well as three eunuchs, and Doihara, Jin Liang, Zheng Xiaoxu, and his son Yan Zuo in disguise, left Tianjin and took a boat to Dalian. (16th)

Tianjin Dispatch: Since Puyi was forced to leave Ping in the 13th year of the Republic of China, he has lived in the Japanese concession in Tianjin for seven years. The Japanese had planned this long ago, thinking that he was a rare commodity and gave him special protection. Two years ago, Puyi originally had the intention of traveling abroad, but he did not succeed because Japanese friends dissuaded him. This time, the Japanese army forcibly occupied Liaoning and Jilin, intending to occupy them permanently. However, in order to take into account international considerations, they had to form a puppet government, actually grasping military and political power themselves. This play cannot be summoned without supporting the deposed emperor Puyi. Therefore, they first sent Doihara to Tianjin. Doihara was very familiar with the situation in China and could speak Chinese. After arriving in Tianjin, he was introduced by Kashii, the Japanese commander in Tianjin, to meet Puyi. Puyi knew that the Japanese side was using him as a temporary puppet, and he was reluctant at first. Doihara repeatedly persuaded him, but he politely declined. Finally, Doihara angrily changed his face, saying, "The Japanese government has protected your safety for several years. Now we want to help you restore the Qing Dynasty, which is really benevolent and righteous. If you don't listen to me, I'm afraid the disaster of killing yourself is at hand. After Puyi was threatened, he asked to discuss it later and discussed the response with his veterans Zheng Xiaoxu, Chen Shichen, and Zhu Yifan. Zheng said that the situation is like this, so he had to follow temporarily. However, Chen and Zhu strongly opposed, saying that if he didn't go, he would die, and if he went, safety would be difficult to guarantee, and he would also lose the sympathy of the Republic of China. Puyi also hesitated. At that time, Puyi's private residence was already under surveillance by the Japanese, and all communication with the outside world was completely lost. After several days of struggle, as a result, he had no choice but to be coerced to Shenyang. At about 12:00 on the evening of the 10th, he led his wife and three eunuchs and set off from his private residence. Zheng Xiaoxu and others also followed, and several armed Japanese soldiers protected them from behind. They arrived at the wharf in the Japanese concession, took a small steamer, and went down the coast through the British and French concessions in the Third Special District and the First Special District, arrived at Tanggu, and changed to the Japanese destroyer Kari. It is now said that he has arrived in Dalian.

The Tianjin Crisis Still Lurks

Although the Tianjin Authorities are Trying to Compromise

The Plainclothes Teams are Still Harassing

Tianjin Dispatch: On the night of the 8th, the plainclothes teams attacked various Chinese institutions from the Japanese concession. For the sake of self-defense, our local police and security teams had no choice but to open fire. Because the plainclothes teams attacked from the Japanese concession, bullets easily flew into the Japanese concession when the security police fired. Therefore, at 5:30 AM on the 9th, when the plainclothes teams were unable to support themselves, the Japanese commander Kashii suddenly protested to our Second Army headquarters by telephone, saying that the Chinese military police (in fact, there was only the security team at that time, no army) opened fire on the Japanese concession and shot and killed several of his officers and soldiers. He should immediately order the military police to retreat 300 meters, otherwise the Japanese army would take necessary measures for self-defense. The so-called necessary measures, in essence, are free action. For the sake of appeasing people and maintaining peace, the provincial and municipal authorities compromised and ordered the police to retreat 300 meters. Unexpectedly, the more we retreated, the more the Japanese pressed on. Not only did the plainclothes teams continue to cause trouble as before, but the 300 meters that had been withdrawn were almost regarded by the Japanese side as an appendage of the Japanese concession, and they interfered with our actions everywhere. The other day, the Japanese consul suddenly proposed to our side that China and Japan jointly inspect the 300-meter area to see if there were any plainclothes teams. The intention of the Japanese side was nothing more than to worry that Britain, the United States, and other countries might advocate demarcating the 300-meter area as a buffer zone. In this case, the Japanese concession would be blockaded by various countries and would not be able to operate. Therefore, on the one hand, they used diplomatic means to deceive various countries with deceptive words. On the other hand, they requested China to jointly search, but they did not know that since the plainclothes teams were under the command of the Japanese, of course they would not stick to being caught. Moreover, this 300-meter area is the complete territory of China, and China has its own discretion whether to search or not. Even if there is a need to search, there is no need for the Japanese side to propose it. However, our authorities actually agreed to the Japanese request and jointly searched. It was originally scheduled to be held at 10:00 AM on the 12th. At that time, our side sent a team of security teams to the gate to discuss the inspection method. The Japanese soldiers glared at each other and refused to inspect. Later, our side questioned the Japanese consul about breaking the appointment. The Japanese consul said that it was not a breach of appointment, but that the translator had made a mistake in the date. It is now scheduled to jointly inspect at 9:00 AM on the 14th. On the morning of the 14th, our side sent 40 security team members, and the Japanese side sent 40 military police, each led by a civil and military official, and divided into two groups. The first group was at the gate, and the second group was at Haiguang Temple.

The Japanese vice consul Goto entertained foreign guests and accompanied them on the tour. His intention was very far-reaching. The first group searched in front of the telephone two bureau door, about 200 meters from the gate. The Japanese pavilion was in an uproar, saying that there should be no defensive works such as telephone networks and sandbags in this area within 300 meters. After our side told them that the telephone bureau was related to the communication of Chinese and foreign people, it could not be without considerable defense. The Japanese side did not understand, so they stopped the inspection. The second group started from Haiguang Temple, but the Japanese side refused to inspect the two districts and six offices occupied by the Japanese army. As a result, the security team only walked on the road and dealt with the matter perfunctorily. Therefore, it was not possible to realize the Japanese soldiers retreating 50 meters and the Chinese and Japanese police resuming their posts as scheduled after the inspection. The Japanese consul used this as an excuse to send a telegram to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs and notify the consuls of various countries stationed in Tianjin, claiming that "Chinese rioters rioted on the night of the 8th of this month and engaged in street battles with Chinese military police. Japanese military officers and Japanese soldiers died by bullets. China accepted the warning of the Japanese consul stationed in Tianjin and retreated beyond 300 meters from the Japanese concession at dawn on the 9th. This is a common sight and sound. However, the Chinese side claims that plainclothes teams have been found in this 300-meter area in recent days. In order to eliminate the rioters, the two sides each sent military police to jointly inspect on the 14th. Defensive works such as telephone networks and sandbags were found in the 300-meter area, which clearly shows that China is not keeping its promises. As a result of the inspection, no trace of plainclothes teams was found, which can prove that Japan has absolutely no protection for rioters. Three security team members were found in the residential houses, who were the ones who shot and killed Japanese officers and soldiers," and so on. On the one hand, they sent a telegram to the Japanese embassy to ask for a protest to our Ministry of Foreign Affairs. On the other hand, they directly protested to the provincial and municipal authorities and asked the municipal government to personally apologize to the Japanese pavilion. Mayor Zhang Xueming had not been able to sleep for a week since the incident occurred, and he suffered from laryngitis. At 6:00 PM on the 14th, he sent representative Ning Xiangnan to the Japanese consulate to explain that Mayor Zhang could not come due to illness. The Japanese consul was unhappy, saying that if he could not come due to illness, he had to make a formal written apology. On the afternoon of the 15th, Zhang sent Liu Jialuan, a counselor of the Second Army, to the Japanese consulate with a letter of apology. Wang Shuchang, on the other hand, went to the Haiguang Temple Japanese barracks at 4:30 PM on the 15th with Shen Dijia Ning Xiangnan to meet with the Japanese commander Kashii. Japanese soldiers surrounded them several times in full armor, with the air of a Hongmen Banquet. At 8:30 PM, Wang was forced to admit the following three conditions: (1) When China and Japan jointly inspected the plainclothes teams on November 14, it was found that there were defensive works within 300 meters of the Japanese concession, and the guns of the security team were facing the Japanese concession. We hereby apologize to the Japanese authorities. (2) Suppress propaganda that is detrimental to Japan's reputation. (3) The defensive works in the 300-meter area will be removed, and the security team will not be allowed to enter this area, but the police may serve with handguns. At 8:40, it was written in Japanese, and Wang signed it before he was able to leave the Japanese barracks and return to the Chinese boundary.

The telephone network in front of the No. 2 Telephone Bureau was actually removed yesterday (15th) afternoon, and the security team also retreated. Our authorities asked the Japanese side to return the two districts and six offices occupied by the Japanese soldiers and to retreat the Japanese soldiers at each intersection 50 meters to restore the posts of the Chinese and Japanese police. The Japanese authorities not only did not agree, but further demanded that our side allocate the Zhongxi Girls' School in the South Guanzitou as the Japanese military office and withdraw the troops 20 miles away. At 10:40 last night, more than 2,000 plainclothes teams were found in the Haiguang Temple area, attacking our line of defense. Our security team was ordered to stop shooting, so they used the telephone to ask the municipal government for instructions. Zhang Xueming immediately telegraphed the Japanese barracks, saying that according to reports, more than 2,000 plainclothes teams were found in the Haiguang Temple area, attacking us very fiercely. For the sake of defense, we must open fire. Please do not misunderstand. Kashii said that whether the security team opens fire or not is up to you, but bullets must not be shot into the Japanese barracks and the Japanese concession. In fact, since the plainclothes teams came out of the Haiguang Temple area and were very close to the Japanese barracks, it would be very easy for stray bullets to fly in if they were counterattacked. Kashii's statement was obviously intended to make things difficult for us. Later, because the plainclothes teams were getting closer and closer, they had directly approached our defense line, and the security team had no choice but to open fire to resist. It was not until 12:30 at night that the rioters were repelled. At 11:30, when the fierce battle was in full swing, the Japanese soldiers opened fire again to cheer them on, and the rumble was deafening. The British, American, and French soldiers defending outside the Qiangzi River heard it all. In short, it has now changed from rioter disturbances to direct contact between China and Japan. The future is bleak, and hidden worries are huge. (16th)

The Inside Story of the Japanese Setting up the Showa Agricultural Company in Shenyang

A Very Poisonous Organization for Seizing Chinese People's Land

Beiping Dispatch: The Japanese organized the Showa Agricultural Company in Shenyang to forcibly occupy the land of the Eastern Provinces and issued thousands of absurd notices. The original text has already been copied in previous reports. Now it is heard that the so-called Showa Agricultural Company was established by Katakura Paper Manufacturing Company with an investment of 50,000 Japanese yen. The managers are Koya Setsuo and Kumagai Kanichi, two former members of the Japanese House of Representatives, who are under the command of the Kwantung Government. In the name of the company, they planned to purchase 60,000 ping of land west of the Fengtian Station on the South Manchuria Railway in preparation for expanding the attached land. The matter was discovered by the authorities, and it was immediately prohibited. Therefore, their plan did not succeed. This was two years ago. Seeing that their plan was not selling, the company spent its money on conspiracy activities to request bribes in order to achieve its goal by any means. However, although the funds were exhausted, no Chinese dared to sell their land. Recently, the company saw that the time had come and obtained the support of the Japanese army. They seized the archives and seals of the Liaoning Finance Office, and then privately forged false contracts and established their own names to transfer the 60,000 ping of land they planned to purchase to the company under the names of the original landowners, and notified the local landowners with printed official letters (as stated in the previous report), ordering them to go to the temporary branch office of the Land Department of the South Manchuria Railway Company to sign new leases and pay taxes according to the regulations. At the same time, they ordered Japanese and Korean ronin to set up markers, delineate boundaries, and have Japanese military police guards. The landowners were terrified because their property was lost in vain. Some went to the so-called temporary branch office of the Land Department of the South Manchuria Railway Company inside the Japanese consulate in Shenyang to register, intending to protect their property in case. However, the Chinese and Japanese personnel in the museum only forced them to sign a lease. There were many conditions in the contract, but they were not allowed to read it, only to sign it, and then drive them out. It is feared that this 60,000 ping of land will soon be transferred into the hands of the Japanese, and the general public will suffer the tragedy of being bankrupted innocently. (16th)

Japanese Communist Party Active in Manchuria

Beiping Correspondence: According to a person who arrived in Beiping from Shenyang a few days ago, on the evening of the 31st of last month, the Manchuria Medical University was suddenly surrounded by Japanese military police who conducted a major search. As a result, more than twenty Japanese students were arrested, causing chaos throughout the school. After inquiries, it was learned that those arrested were suspected of being communists. It is said that these students, having received higher education, were ideologically clear-headed and extremely dissatisfied with their country's dispatch of troops to the Northeast and occupation of Liaoning and Jilin. They planned to unite and take action, but the plan was leaked to the school authorities, who reported it to the Japanese military, leading to their arrest. In my opinion, since the Northeast Incident, the Japanese Communist Party has also taken the opportunity of their country's troops occupying Liaoning and Jilin to enter Manchuria. Their primary task is to complete the organization of the Japanese Communist Party's Manchuria Local Affairs Bureau. The headquarters is located in Dalian, with four departments: organization, propaganda, technology, and countermeasures. Each department has a director, with seven people including Matsui Takashi as the leaders. Each department also has a liaison system and other labor organizations. The content is very tight and the foundation is very stable. There are about a hundred party members in total, led by another party member, Matsushima, who are carrying out various activities. Their methods are extremely clever. All party members, except for particularly urgent meetings, usually live scattered in remote inns or Japanese residences. They dress elegantly and act discreetly. The work of the technical department is more important, so female party members are assigned to it. The "Manchuria Red Flag" newspaper, published in Fushun, serves as their propaganda organ. It is published twice a month, privately printed by party members using mimeograph, and includes illustrations. The content is highly stimulating and widely distributed. Local branches have also been actively organized in the past month, and are largely complete. They originally planned to take advantage of the Labor Revolution Memorial Day on November 7th to unite with the Korean Communist Party and local bandits to launch a coordinated uprising. However, the plan was leaked and detected by the Japanese police, who first exposed the "Manchuria Red Flag" by the Fushun Japanese Police Station on the 26th of last month. On the 28th, the Dalian Police Station's Ideological Higher Education Department, in cooperation with various detectives, conducted a major search in Dalian. On the 31st, Manchuria Medical University was also searched, and other places followed suit. As a result, more than thirty members of the Japanese Communist Party were arrested, but important leaders such as Matsui Takashi and Matsushima Kan escaped, and many important documents were destroyed. It is said that when the Communist Party in Dalian was exposed, some even fought the police with handguns. Because many of the participants were excellent, their intentions and designs were very meticulous. Although they have suffered this blow, they seem to have suffered no major losses. (16th)

Qingdao Situation Suddenly Turns Serious

Japanese Ronin Group's Attempted Disturbance in Plainclothes Fails

Japanese Destroyer Fleet Arrives in Qingdao to Demonstrate

Jiaoji Railway Defense Consolidated, No Other Concerns

Qingdao Correspondence: When the Japanese expatriates in this city held the Shandong Residents' General Meeting at the end of last month, they resolved to make efforts to create a major incident. Since then, they have proceeded according to the resolution, creating trouble everywhere. However, our government, merchants, and people all understand their intentions and are taking strict precautions to avoid conflict. At present, the Japanese are working harder to create incidents in order to provoke negotiations and use this as an excuse to send troops. Therefore, the situation in this city has suddenly become tense in recent days. All shops close early every night, and there are no pedestrians on the streets around 10 p.m. The Public Security Bureau has also imposed martial law in an invisible way, assigning more double guards. The night security team's bicycle team is fully mobilized, deploying in important locations in the city. Each person is issued two hundred bullets for use in case of emergencies. At the important intersections outside the city, the Marine Corps has stationed heavy troops, so the Japanese have no chance to take advantage of, and peace has been maintained. It is said that the Japanese ronin, unable to achieve their goals, have turned to buying Chinese coolies to serve as plainclothes teams, giving each person 200 yuan and multiple bombs. The original plan was to have them bomb various important institutions at night, and the Japanese ronin would then attack in order to cause major negotiations. Unexpectedly, this was discovered by the Public Security Bureau, which took strict precautions in advance. The plainclothes team, intimidated by the force, did not dare to launch an attack. However, the city has been alarmed several times overnight, giving the impression that disaster is imminent.

The Japanese 13th Destroyer Squadron, including the "Hatsukari," "Hayanae," "Kuretake," and "Wakatake" arrived in Qingdao this morning (16th) at 8:50 a.m. from Lushun to demonstrate, and are anchored in the front sea with the flagship "Kuma," ready to be launched at any time, attracting more attention. The details of the four ships are investigated as follows:

Ship Name　Displacement　Number of People　Captain

Hatsukari　900 tons　101 people　Lieutenant Commander Kengo Kadota

Hayanae　Same as above　Same as above　Lieutenant Commander Masao Tachibana

Kuretake　Same as above　Same as above　Lieutenant Commander Masayuki Kitamura

Wakatake　Same as above　Same as above　Lieutenant Commander Tsuneo Kuranaga

Ge Guangting, Chairman of the Jiaoji Railway Committee, because of the tense situation and the extreme importance of the Jiaoji Railway's defense, went to Jinan the day before yesterday to discuss with Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Provincial Government, methods for maintaining the Jiaoji Railway's security. The matter has now been completed, and he returned to Qingdao at 7:30 this morning (16th). According to Ge, the defense along the Jiaoji Railway line is jointly undertaken by the 3rd Route Army and the railway police, and it is now consolidated, with no other concerns. (November 16th)

Fujian Authorities Strictly Prevent Japanese Riots

Fuzhou Correspondence: Acting Chairman Fang Shengtao recently received orders to go to Beijing, and yesterday received a telegram from Beijing stating that recently in Shanghai and Tianjin, Japanese rioters have combined to cause trouble, but they have been suppressed and dispersed by the military and police, and local order has been restored immediately. However, the rioters had secretly colluded with thugs in advance, hid in the interior, and took the opportunity to riot. Fujian must take strict precautions to prevent trouble from arising. After receiving the telegram, the provincial government convened a meeting on the 13th with Martial Law Deputy Commander Li Dingzhang, 1st Brigade Commander Jin Zhenzhong, 2nd Brigade Commander Zhou Xiaopei, and Municipal Public Security Bureau Chief Guo Yongrong, and resolved to intensify martial law starting that evening, and ordered the martial law department's inspection team, the Public Security Bureau's district offices, and the security and detective teams to divide the area and deploy strictly.

Wuhu's Large Quantities of Rapeseed Still Shipped to Japan

A Recent Overview of Chinese and Foreign Shipping in the Yangtze River

Wuhu Correspondence: Rice and rapeseed are the main agricultural products of Anhui Province. Wuhu is a treaty port and a major export hub, and its foreign trade is considerable. According to recent news from shipping circles, since the invasion of Liaoning and Jilin by the violent Japanese, of the nine merchant ships of Japanese registry sailing on the Yangtze River, four are used to transport Japanese expatriates, while the other five are docked in Shanghai, where Chinese ships load cargo. Currently, the Chinese ships engaged in Yangtze River shipping include the China Merchants Bureau's "Jianghua," "Jiang'an," "Jiangshun," "Jiangxin," "Jiangda," "Jing," and "Jianguo." Wuhu's current imports are mostly seafood, etc., so the China Merchants Bureau's cargo ships are piled high with goods, about 10,000 pieces in total. Because they cannot be shipped in time, the Wuhu branch has telegraphed the head office to request a temporary suspension of shipments. Exports are mostly miscellaneous goods, all wholesale from various counties. In addition, the Sanbei Company's "Xinning," "Xingchang," "Xingshi," "Chang'an," "Dexing," and "Ningshao" vessels also sail on the Yangtze River. Previously, business was very dull, but in the past two weeks, because the China Merchants Bureau's passenger and cargo ships were overcrowded, they have also been greatly boosted. Before the Northeast Incident occurred, Japanese ships had a significant advantage in business, carrying mainly rapeseed and rapeseed cake to Japan. According to customs statistics, from April to September of this year, the rapeseed and rapeseed cake transported from Wuhu to Japan were as follows:

Month　Rapeseed Packages　Rapeseed Cake Pieces

April　42,949　7,319

May　2,670　None

June　14,827　None

July　63,899　4,226

August　57,684　4,893

September　8,496　None

In total, there were 163,525 packages of rapeseed (each package weighing 140 catties) and 16,438 pieces of rapeseed cake. Previously, when shipping to Japan, Japanese ships were exclusively used unless absolutely necessary. If a foreign ship was occasionally reported, the Japanese merchants would insist on returning and replacing it with a Japanese ship, which shows how well the Japanese promoted nationalized industries. Now, since September 22nd, Taikoo and Jardine have been used for shipments. However, all sectors in Wuhu believe that shipping so much rapeseed to Japan provides the enemy with raw materials, which conflicts with the principle of economic disengagement. The County Rectification Committee has convened various sectors to hold a meeting this afternoon to discuss this issue. (16th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

During the winter defense period, bandits contemplate action. Wu Daoli, a man from Nanjing who operates a tannery outside Niangniang Temple north of Kuatang Bridge in the western suburbs of this city, suddenly heard violent knocking on the door around 1 a.m. yesterday (17th). Wu's son was ill, and many relatives and friends were watching by his bedside. The bandits heard the loud voices inside and knew it would be difficult to succeed, so they fired a shot and left. The relatives and friends opened the door and chased after them, but their shadows disappeared in the dark. Five suspects were apprehended along the way, but after inquiries, it was learned that they were farmers selling rice straw and had no connection to the bandits.

The new Construction Bureau Director takes office. Sun Shengzu, Director of the Construction Bureau of this county, has been ordered to transfer to the Shanghai County Construction Bureau. Xu Baikui, a member of the Provincial Committee, will succeed him in this county and also serve as Director of the Tanggong Office. The new Director Xu arrived in Songjiang on the 17th to take office.

Kunshan

Autumn harvest yield rate agreed upon. The autumn harvest yield rate of this county was previously surveyed twice in the countryside by the district offices, farmers' associations, and local gentry. The average calculation for the entire county is only 47%, which is far from the 70% set by the Provincial Department. Yesterday, the Finance and Agriculture Departments specially sent Weng Youcheng and Huang Xizhou to Kunshan. The county government immediately convened a meeting of district chiefs, bureau chiefs, and representatives of various groups to discuss the issue. The two commissioners reported on the autumn harvest yield rates of various counties and the province's urgent need for funds. After the public explained the severity of this year's disaster to the Provincial Committee, the result was set at 60%.

Suzhou

Water police search and suppress lake bandits who robbed boats. The small steamboat from Jiaxing to Xinshi was attacked by bandits the day before yesterday when passing through the Shanghegang area of Xiushui County, Zhejiang Province, in Taihu Lake. Fourteen passengers were kidnapped. The details have already been reported in the newspaper. It is now known that four of the kidnapped hostages have been released. The 15th Team of the 3rd District and the 10th Team of the 2nd District of the water police have all set out and are heading to Taihu Lake to search and suppress the bandits. It is said that the bandits have now fled to the Qingpu area.

Wuxi

Water police capture communists. The 2nd Division of the 6th Team of the 2nd District of the water police, based on a secret report, captured two notorious bandits in a thatched shed near Pujiqiao near Beitang Fudian, and seized a handgun. According to their confessions, there are still accomplices hiding in Qingshan Bay. Team Leader Sun has led the police to investigate overnight. Furthermore, Team Leader Tan Shuren of the 3rd Division captured three male and female bandits in the Jiufeng Workshop the day before yesterday (17th): one named Wang Kaitang, also known as Wang Xiuzi, one named Yin Xueguan, and the woman named Wang Zhushi. According to their confessions, they used to work with the Communist Party in Taixing, where there were many party members. They have one submachine gun, two Mauser pistols, and one handgun, all in Taixing. Last year, they committed a robbery and received 53 yuan. They recently fled to Wuxi. On the 30th of last month, they gathered accomplices to discuss a plan to rob large shops in the Beitang area. Wang Zhushi became acquainted with them after arriving in Wuxi and was unaware of the plan. After receiving the confession, Team Leader Tan ordered the two bandits Wang and Yin to be handed over to the district for interrogation. Wang Zhushi was released on bail.

Assaulting the police case heard in court yesterday. Xia Chungang, Chief of the 16th Branch of the Public Security Bureau, sent police officers Meng Qingfa and eight others to catch gamblers in Zhu A'da teahouse in Yangting Town, 8th District, last month. However, Gao Yiqing and Deng Zuobi, the Deputy Chiefs of the town, dared to instigate the gamblers to beat the police officers, causing injuries. Police Officer Meng was the most seriously injured and died the next day. After an autopsy by the court, the accomplices Zhu Zhongfen and Li Genquan were arrested and detained. It is now known that yesterday (18th) was the date for the court to hear the case. Meng Sunshi, Meng Xiande, Xia Chungang, and Du Xizhen were present. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Yang opened the court, questioned them, and ordered Meng Sunshi to be dismissed. Xia Chungang and Du Xizhen were released on bail pending further investigation.

Wujiang

Suzhou boat robbed again. Yesterday (16th) at 1 p.m., the Majinfu boat from Suzhou to Wujiang was suddenly stopped by a bandit boat in Guajing Port. Eight bandits with guns, speaking in local dialect, jumped on board and robbed the passengers, the boat's silver, goods, clothes, bedding, and goods carried by the shops, worth about four or five hundred yuan in total. They disembarked, set sail, and headed towards Taihu Lake.

Jiangyin

Party Ideology Teacher Fakes Credentials. The Executive Committee of the First District Party Department, in view of the fact that Jiang Liquan of Jiangyin (currently a candidate for the county executive committee), a Party Ideology Teacher who was examined and qualified by the Jiangsu Provincial Party Ideology Teacher Examination Committee, had fabricated his academic qualifications (claiming to have graduated from Peking University and worked as a teacher at Shanghai Minli Middle School and Wuxi Jingzhi Girls' Middle School), as Jiang is a nurse from the Red Swastika Society and passed the examination to become a judicial clerk in the county government, how could he deceive? A decision was made at a meeting the day before yesterday to submit the case to the higher party department for verification.

Changzhou

Notorious bandit Shen Yuanxing apprehended. Shen Yuanxing, an accomplice of Qin Er'gou, a notorious bandit who has already been executed in Wuyi County, has committed many kidnapping and robbery cases in the 4th and 5th Districts, and his crimes are unforgivable. Recently, due to the authorities' strict search and arrest, Shen fled to Shanghai. The county government sent a detective team to Shanghai to investigate. It was learned that the bandit had changed his name to Shu Wuda and was hiding at No. 144 Fuqing Lane, Tangjia Lane, Shanghai. The Shanghai Concession Police were immediately contacted and he was arrested. Zhang County Chief, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered Ni Gusheng, the Detective Team Leader, to lead the detectives to Shanghai on the 18th to bring him back for interrogation.

Zhenjiang

Yizheng County representatives come to the province to petition. All butchers in Yizheng County have gone on strike because Zhao Liancheng, the tax collector for the county's slaughter tax, collects taxes without receipts and collects multiple times with one receipt. Furthermore, the police of the county's Public Security Bureau listen to Zhao's false accusations of tax resistance and arbitrarily detain good butchers, causing great harassment. Yesterday, Chen Naichen and Wu Bingchen, the Supervisory Committee members of the county's Chamber of Commerce, came to the province on behalf of the butchers, carrying a petition to the Provincial Government and the Department of Civil Affairs this morning. Yao Bichen, a staff member of the Provincial Government's Public Relations Section, received them on behalf of the government, and Lin Wenqin, the section chief of the Department of Civil Affairs, received them. The results were satisfactory. The prefecture will forward the petition to the department, ordering the county to investigate and respond.

The Provincial Model Factory will be restored. The site of the Provincial Model Silk Weaving Factory is located at Meijiaqiao, Panmen, Suzhou, and was rebuilt from the old copper coin bureau. It has been closed for many years. Part of the buildings was allocated by the former department head to the Rehabilitation Institute for use, and another part was used to store machinery. It was found that there were still newly purchased machines that had not been installed. Upon taking office, Director Shen immediately ordered the technicians and the Fourth Section to jointly plan for the disposal of the machinery to avoid rust and abandonment. Recently, Meng Zubei presented a plan, stating that Jiangsu is rich in silk production and there is a need to promote and improve silk weaving. He requested that the factory buildings be repaired, additional machinery be added, and the factory be restored quickly. He also submitted separate budgets for expenditures and revenues, claiming that an allocation of 10,000 yuan would be enough to start work, and that the annual output would be sold for 195,500 yuan, with a profit of over 8,000 yuan after deducting expenses. Director Shen found the submitted plan insightful and has instructed Section Chief Jin and Technician Wu to review it.

Please thoroughly resolve the obstructing water dikes. The previous Zhenjiang Yantai Taidongxing Flood Relief Association reported that the Yun dike had collapsed, turning five counties into a swamp. The dikes of the downstream salt reclamation companies were blocking the water from entering the sea, causing extreme danger. They jointly petitioned the provincial government, and Commissioner Li Mingyang of the provincial government led a team to open the dikes, as previously reported. When Commissioner Li set out, the association publicly selected Shen Linsen, a flood victim, to accompany him as a guide. Now, Mr. Shen has reported the progress of the handling to the association and has drafted four measures to thoroughly resolve the problem: (1) order the downsizing of districts, (2) order the widening of river channels, (3) dredge the existing river channels, and (4) open the tributaries of the Doulong Port. After discussion, the association considered these measures extremely important and has submitted them to the provincial government, ordering the salt reclamation companies to promptly seek remedies.

Relief for unemployed silk factory workers. The Weilun Silk Factory has not resumed operations after receiving the maintenance public bonds. The unemployed workers, concerned about their livelihood, have repeatedly requested relief from the party and government organs, but Zhang Shaoqin, the factory manager, has avoided appearing. The county party and government organs have now decided on a solution, ordering the factory to resume operations. The county party department, the county government, and the Public Security Bureau will supervise the start of operations, which should continue until the 17,000 yuan in public bonds have been exhausted, after which the factory will be allowed to close. The public bonds should be deposited in a bank by the factory, with certification from the county party department, the county government, and the Public Security Bureau. If the factory still fails to start operations within ten days, the three organs will devise a solution.

Nantong

Court reorganization and upgrade issues. The Nantong County Court has been ordered to reorganize and upgrade to a District Court to facilitate appeals of civil and criminal cases from various counties in northern Jiangsu. The required funding of 10,000 yuan must be raised locally. President Jian, facing difficulties in proceeding, has gone to the High Court for instructions.

Yangzhou

The teacher debt collection tide remains difficult to resolve. All social education institutions and small schools in Jiangdu have been on strike for ten days, and there is still no solution to the issue of unpaid salaries. Therefore, they have each selected representatives, wearing symbols, and gathered at the Education Bureau to sit and demand their salaries. By nightfall, there was still no resolution, so Inspector Liu Yin'nan came out to persuade them to return temporarily. On the morning of the 17th, they returned to the Education Bureau to sit and demand their salaries. It is said that Director Ning has no solution either and plans to visit the county magistrate for instructions. However, the parents of the students, concerned that the long strike will completely deprive their children of education, plan to form a joint association of parents of children from various schools, notify all parents, and schedule a public lecture at the Ma Shen Temple public lecture hall at 2 p.m. on the 22nd to discuss an appropriate maintenance plan.

Educational News

Important News

No Need to Establish a Special Department for National Arts

Ministry of Education Responds to Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee

The Ministry of Education stated that since national arts have already been designated as one of the practical matters in the physical education curriculum, there is no need to establish a separate department. It responded to the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee's letter as follows: "The letter from your office, forwarded by the Henan Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee, based on the request of the Kaifeng County Party Department, to list national arts as a required subject in all schools below the senior middle school level, has been approved for review by the Ministry of Education." After investigation, since national arts are one of the practical matters in the physical education curriculum, and have already been stipulated in the Ministry's standards for primary and secondary school physical education, there is no need to establish a separate department. The letter has been sent to the appropriate parties for their information.

(4) Japan's recent attitude towards China: (A) Proposing international co-management (international police as a prelude to international co-management), (B) Carrying out bombardment of Heilongjiang, (C) Now viewing the Tanaka policy as preparing for permanent occupation of the three eastern provinces. (5) The attitude we should take recently: (A) Japan does not abide by the resolutions of the League of Nations Administrative Council, and the people of the whole country should rise up urgently to carry out effective self-defense within the time limit for troop withdrawal, (B) The people of the whole country should rise up urgently to aid the Heilongjiang army and strive to resist Japan to the end, (C) Unanimously request the government to immediately declare war on Japan, (D) China should immediately withdraw from the League of Nations, which cannot prevent Japan's rampant brutality, (E) The people of the whole country should rise up urgently and unanimously, arm themselves, and vow to restore lost territory with iron and blood.

City Education Bureau Bans the Private Jianye Automobile School

The Education News Agency reports that after the City Education Bureau sent personnel to investigate the private Jianye Automobile School, it was determined that the facilities were simple and that the school did not pay attention to academic theory, only teaching driving skills, which was purely the nature of a training center. The school was ordered to quickly correct its school name, articles of association, and organizational content, and that the tuition fees charged should also be reduced. However, the school has not yet made any changes. Recently, it was reported that the school's students filed a complaint that the school was overcharging tuition fees and that the advertisements published were fraudulent. The bureau then reiterated its previous order and strictly limited the school to amend its school name and articles of association before November 30, effectively reduce tuition fees, and then apply for registration. Otherwise, the school will be closed.

Shanghai Middle School Experimental Primary School's Exhibit at the Belgian International Exposition Wins Gold Medal Award

Student's Japanese Studies Works

When Belgium celebrated the centenary of its independence and held an International Exposition, the Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School Experimental Primary School, in accordance with the orders of the Ministry and the Provincial Department, selected and submitted the Japanese studies works of the primary school students and all the teaching materials of the unit, totaling more than 200 items, to the Provincial Department and then to the Ministry. They were subsequently selected for exhibition at the Belgian Exposition, and the representative office was permitted to donate them to the Belgian government for permanent display in museums or libraries, as previously reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that the school recently received a letter from the representative office of the National Government participating in the Belgian Exposition, stating that the exhibit won a gold medal and that a representative will be sent to attend the award ceremony held at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on November 28.

The Champion Team of Gibraltar

│The Northambert Leaves Shanghai on Monday│

Negotiating for Guangdong to Elect the Fourth Central Committee Members Early

Chen Mingshu, a representative from Beijing, is negotiating with representatives from Guangdong for the election of the fourth Central Committee members and discussing important cases related to domestic and foreign affairs because the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee in Beijing is scheduled to close on the 22nd of this month. Details of the discussions and contents are recorded below.
