The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is Preparing to Send Ships to Japan to Carry Overseas Chinese.

The Xinwan was Scheduled to Depart for Yokohama.

Departure will take place once a reply telegram is received.

Order from the Ministry to Send Ships. Since the start of the Anti-Japanese War, overseas Chinese in Japan have been returning to China. In the past two months, about eight or nine thousand people have come to Shanghai. However, there are still over a thousand compatriots in Tokyo, Yokohama, and other places who are unable to afford passage. They have requested our ambassador to Japan to rescue them and return them to their home country. The embassy sent a telegram to the central government requesting that ships be sent to transport them. The Ministry of Communications sent a telegram to Shanghai ordering the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to send one or two ships to Japan to rescue the overseas Chinese and return them to Shanghai as soon as possible.

The Company Telegraphically Inquired About the Procedures. After receiving the telegram from the Ministry, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company sent a return telegram to the Ministry stating that the company did not have its own docks in Japan and had no experience operating ships there. For this trip to Japan, the number of overseas Chinese, food supplies, preparations, hiring local江 at the time of arrival, and negotiating with the docks must be completed in advance to avoid any obstructions. The Ministry was requested to inform the embassy or consulate in Japan to handle the arrangements. Once a reply telegram was received, the ship could depart.

The Xin Feng Ship was Scheduled. General Manager Guo and the Business Department discussed the matter yesterday and decided that, since it concerned an order from the Ministry, it had to be carried out. Initially, it was planned to send the Xinming ship. However, since it was carrying a large amount of cargo to Tianjin, the ship had already departed and would not be able to go to Japan until the 30th of this month. Since that date was too late, it was decided to send the Xin Feng ship to Yokohama instead. The ship is currently under repair and will depart as soon as it leaves the dock. The Ministry has already been notified.

Telegraph to Japan to Handle Procedures. Yesterday morning, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company sent a telegram to the Consul-General in Yokohama to inquire about the number of overseas Chinese and the entry, exit, and docking procedures for the ship upon arrival in Japan. Since the company's ships did not have passenger ship licenses for foreign voyages, it was necessary to obtain them before departure. After sending this telegram, the company received a reply telegram from Consul Zhou in Yokohama in the afternoon, which only stated that there were over a thousand overseas Chinese waiting to be transported but did not mention any procedures upon arrival. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company considered the matter to be of great importance and did not want to act hastily. Another telegram was sent in the afternoon to inquire further. The departure date will be determined after a reply is received. According to a company insider, the departure should take place within two or three days.

Wu Chao-shu on the League of Nations

It is not yet time to hope that the League of Nations will help the weak and eliminate the strong.

We should not be overly disappointed as a matter of fact.

We should understand its strength and use it well.

In recent days, the Manchurian Incident has relied almost entirely on the League of Nations to resolve it. The League of Nations Administrative

Page 14

The academy is holding a meeting in Paris. All Chinese people have great hopes for the League of Nations. Reporters from various news agencies believed that Mr. Wu Yunti had twice been the chief representative of China to the League of Nations and had also served as the vice-chairman of the League of Nations. He should know the inside story of the League of Nations, so they visited him and recorded his conversation. Wu said, "There are two types of people in the world who are not good friends of the League of Nations: those who look down on the League of Nations and those who value it too much. If we want to discuss the League of Nations calmly, we should first understand how much power the League of Nations has, and then we will know how to use the League of Nations well. We must know that the League of Nations is not a government, listed alongside other countries in the world, and especially not a supreme government above the governments of other countries. One point is easiest to prove: on October 24, the League of Nations Administrative Council had a resolution limiting Japan to withdraw its Manchurian army to the South Manchuria Railway by November 16. After unanimous passage by the representatives of various countries, the Japanese representative did not approve. Therefore, although this proposal has great power in public opinion, it has no legal effect. Someone asked me, 'Why does the League of Nations Charter stipulate this way? One country's opposition makes the resolution ineffective?' I replied that all resolutions of the League of Nations, except those concerning procedural issues, must be unanimously passed before they take effect. Because each country is an independent and autonomous country, the League of Nations is not a supreme government, and countries cannot listen to its orders. The League of Nations has a very important mission, which is to uphold world justice and maintain world peace. Needless to say, this mission requires an extremely powerful mechanism to bear it. To be honest, the League of Nations in thirty years may be able to bear it, but the League of Nations today is not certain. We must know that the governments of all countries in the world have a long history, some for thousands of years, and others for a hundred or so years. The League of Nations has only been twelve years old since it was born this year. It has no soldiers of its own, and not even money. Its expenses are entirely provided by member states. Not only do countries not listen to the orders of the League of Nations, but the League of Nations should not look at the nose of the countries. Although the League of Nations has a general assembly and an administrative council, behind it there is also a secretariat, secretly manipulating the power of the right and left, and the power of the secretariat is in the hands of two or three strong countries. With this kind of reason, if two weak countries have disputes and appeal to the League of Nations, the League of Nations may be able to uphold justice. If two strong countries have disputes, the League of Nations already feels that it is difficult to be a person. However, it may still be able to uphold justice. If one strong and one weak have disputes, it is difficult to hope that it will uphold justice. We cannot be disappointed in the League of Nations because of this, but we can only say that it does not have this power today, hoping that others will have this power on their own. A twelve-year-old child is asked to lift a thousand pounds, and the child cannot lift it. It is not the child's fault, but the order is immeasurable. Someone said, 'Does the League of Nations Charter stipulate that there is a method of economic绝交? Is it possible to achieve it?' However, the resolution of the League of Nations is the resolution of each member. If Britain, France, Italy, Germany, and other countries are unwilling to make significant sacrifices and use this fierce method to deal with Japan, then the League of Nations will not have a resolution of economic绝交. So what ability and what role does this twelve-year-old League of Nations have? In my opinion, there are three points: (1) Propaganda effect. The League of Nations is the world's agency, and the world's newspapers often send reporters to Geneva. When there are important meetings, reporters are temporarily sent again. There are three or four hundred newspapers around the world that send commissioners. Therefore, the League of Nations can be used as the world's largest broadcasting station. If there is something unfair, appeal to the League of Nations, and the whole world will hear it, which can issue a mobilization order to world opinion. (2) When the General Assembly and the Administrative Council of the League of Nations are held, the world's great politicians and diplomats will come here. Representatives of various countries can associate with each other from morning to night, and discuss with each other. They can make private friendships, and they can solve international outstanding cases. Therefore, the League of Nations is a good talking room. (3) In addition to politics and diplomacy, countries around the world have many common relationships, such as drug prevention, hygiene, science, and protection of women and children, which cannot be won. The League of Nations promotes or presides over it, so the League of Nations can be said to be the world's chain. At present, the role of the League of Nations is these three. It is hoped that it will uphold justice, help the weak and eliminate the strong, which is at least a matter of twenty years. It is not yet talked about today. In the past, there were many people in China who looked down on the League of Nations, because they did not understand the three functions of the League of Nations mentioned above. Recently, there are many people in China who value the League of Nations too much, thinking that the cause of twenty years can be done by the League of Nations today. When the League of Nations cannot do it, they are greatly disappointed. Therefore, from the people who value the League of Nations too much, they will inevitably become people who look down on the League of Nations too much. So I say that the two types of people are not good friends of the League of Nations. Since China is one of the member states, the Chinese people should understand the ability of the League of Nations and the limits of its ability. They should not expect too much, and they should not despise it and ignore it. At the same time, they should also study the method of using the League of Nations well. They should not abuse it, and they should not be used by it. This is the obligation that national diplomacy should have.

Seventy-Eighth Division Commander Qu Shounian Arrives in Shanghai

After the Nineteenth Route Army was ordered to arrive in the Nanjing-Shanghai area to undertake garrison duties, it was decided that the entire Seventy-Eighth Division would be stationed in Shanghai. Advance personnel arrived from Xunyang a few days ago to arrange everything. The commander of the Seventy-Eighth Division, Qu Shounian, also arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing the evening before last (the 17th) and arrived here at eight o'clock this morning to discuss the division's stationing locations with local Shanghai authorities. A reporter from the New Sound News Agency interviewed Commander Qu's aide, Mr. Yu, yesterday to inquire about various news items, and received the following answers:

The Garrison Commander Position Decided to Be Succeeded by Dai Ji: Regarding the Shanghai-Woosung Garrison Commander issue, after Xiong Shihui completed the handover, the central government considered the Shanghai-Woosung defense to be of great importance and that a leader should not be lacking for even a day. Initially, Jiang Guangnai was considered to succeed him, but Jiang strongly declined. Subsequently, there was an order for the newly appointed Nanjing-Shanghai Garrison Commander Chen Mingshu to temporarily hold the position concurrently. However, Chen also felt that although Nanjing and Shanghai were close, it was still difficult to provide adequate command due to the distance. Therefore, it was decided that Dai Ji, the chief of staff of the Nineteenth Route Army, would succeed him. Dai is now preparing to come to Shanghai within a few days. However, his assumption of office will take place after the Fourth Plenary Session concludes and Chen Mingshu assumes office as the Nanjing-Shanghai Garrison Commander.

The Seventy-Eighth Division Comes to Shanghai via Xunyang and Nanjing: After receiving the order to lead his troops to Shanghai for garrison duty, Qu Shounian, the commander of the Seventy-Eighth Division, immediately issued an order for the troops to assemble in Jiujiang to await transportation by ship to Nanjing. Without delay, they will proceed to Shanghai for garrison duty. Their stationing locations will be approximately as follows: the Second Regiment will be stationed in Zhabei and Jiangwan, which will be guarded by the division's special service battalion, and the remaining troops will be stationed in the Longhua Temple area.

Kunshan Garrison Troops Arrived Yesterday: Kunshan is located in a crucial area between Nanjing and Shanghai. Given the current national crisis, defense should be taken with particular care. Chen Mingshu has decided that the Sixtieth Division and the Sixty-First Supplementary Brigade of the Nineteenth Route Army will be responsible for the garrison. These troops arrived in Kunshan yesterday morning from Nanjing. With this tight arrangement, the security of Nanjing and Shanghai can be ensured.

Yesterday's News on Resisting Japan and Saving the Nation

Letter Reported That Customs Brokers Are Forbidden to Load Goods on Japanese Ships: The Anti-Japanese Association previously received confidential reports that customs brokers were secretly loading goods onto Japanese ships. After investigation, it was found that there were many small customs brokers in Nanshi that were not members of the public association, making it impossible to take action against them for the time being. Yesterday, a letter was sent to the Customs Brokers Association, stating: "Regarding the case of customs brokers secretly loading goods onto Japanese ships, which has been reported, after the Association dispatched the Investigation Department to investigate, the reply was received stating that the Zhen Da Customs Brokerage on Lao Yong'an Street claimed that they did load goods to Osaka previously, but not since September 15th. Upon reviewing the overseas shipping records, this was confirmed. An investigation was also conducted at the Fuxingheng Customs Brokerage in Chang Geng Lane on Avenue Edward VII, which claimed that they have not shipped any goods since the 22nd of last month. The medicinal materials and other items were indeed loaded at the Mitsubishi Wharf, and the customs declarations for these goods were handled by Japanese customs brokers. They requested that the Association take severe action. An inquiry was made with the Nanshi Customs Brokers Association, which stated that they could only forward a warning to each firm after receiving a letter from this Association. However, it seems that there is no way to deal with the small customs brokers who are not members of the public association, as they account for six out of ten. Therefore, it is reported that economic severance is the only way to save the nation, and it is the consensus of the entire nation. All customs brokers are citizens, yet they dare to disregard public opinion and continue to declare and load goods on Japanese ships, undermining the anti-Japanese movement. We do not know what their intentions are. We hereby request your Association to investigate and forward a warning to all colleagues that they must not declare and load goods on Japanese ships in the future. Otherwise, once discovered, they will be severely punished. This is addressed to the Customs Brokers Association."

Prohibition of Japanese Exclusive Films Being Shown in China: The Anti-Japanese Association issued its 16th public notice yesterday, stating: "It has been secretly reported that a large number of films exclusively owned by the Japanese Towa Trading Co. in China, such as 'The Blue Angel', 'The Last Squad', 'White Devil', 'A Trip to the Moon', 'Immortal Elves', 'Beauty Pass', 'A Dream Hard to Fulfill', 'Spiritual and Physical Conflict', 'Love at Sea', etc., will be successively screened in various theaters in Shanghai, and managed by Manager Luo of a certain film company. Ostensibly, they are using the name of the Chinese Wufa Film Company, but in reality, all the profits go to the Japanese. This is extremely hateful. At this time of national crisis, we are eager to contribute money to alleviate the difficulties, and we fear that it is not enough. How can we use the money to save the country to fill the pockets of our enemies? We hereby urgently notify all Chinese cinemas in the city not to screen the above-mentioned films. All Chinese with blood and spirit should not buy tickets to watch the above-mentioned films. We fear that this may not be widely known, so we hereby issue this notice."

The Yidu Ship Was Completely Blown Up

Four Deaths in the Engine Room

Cargo Ship Loss Valued at 500,000

Cause of the Disaster: The Yidu ship, owned by the American company Yangtze Rapids Steamship Co., operating on the Shanghai-Chongqing line, was carrying cargo from Shanghai to Chongqing. On the morning of the 17th of this month, when sailing to the Yangdu Bay area upstream of Fuzhou, the cylinder in the engine room suddenly exploded. The nearby oil storage ship was also damaged by the explosion, and gasoline flowed out and into the engine room. Once exposed to the heat, a tragic accident occurred with a loud explosion.

Crew Casualties: At the time, Chief Engineer Zhang Yueming, stokers, and others were working in the engine room. They were unable to escape in time and were all killed in the explosion. It has been reported that at least four people were killed in the engine room. The other injured firemen are still being investigated. After the accident, the ship sailed into a shallow area and grounded itself to facilitate rescue.

Passengers Rescued: The passengers inside the ship panicked and tried to escape, with more than 20 people jumping into the river. Fortunately, the river was shallow, preventing them from drowning. The shipowner urgently sent a telegram for help. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Emei ship was the first to receive the telegram and immediately sailed to the area, rescuing the passengers onto its ship and taking them to Chongqing. Therefore, there were no casualties among the passengers, which was fortunate amidst the misfortune.

Warship Assisted in Rescue: The American gunboat USS Tutuila, stationed upstream of Yichang, received the ship's distress call and immediately sailed to Yangdu Bay to assist in the rescue. All the captain, crew, and sailors were rescued by the warship. Two telegrams were sent yesterday reporting that rescue efforts were still underway.

Cargo Ship Completely Destroyed: The ship was fully loaded with over 200 pieces of textiles, over 400 bags of white sugar, and 700-800 pieces of miscellaneous goods from Shanghai. After the explosion, the entire ship caught fire. Yesterday, the Shanghai office received a telegram from the American warship stating that all the cargo on the ship had been completely burned and nothing remained.

Aftermath: A reporter visited the company yesterday to inquire. The person in charge replied that the hull could be salvaged, and the machinery, except for the boiler, could still be used. They would try to tow the ship back to Shanghai. The ship had a displacement of 600 tons and cost 300,000 taels to build. It was insured for 250,000 taels with the American Asia Insurance Company in Shanghai. Most of the cargo was insured. The passengers have been notified. The total loss is estimated to be over 500,000 yuan.

Yuanshun Ship Hit a Reef and Then Collided with an American Warship

Stranded on a Reef in Quanzhou: The Yuanshun ship, owned by the Yingkou Dalian Company and operating along the coast, loaded cargo from Niuzhuang to Fujian and was unloading in Quanzhou. On the morning of the 14th of this month, after unloading all the cargo from Quanzhou, it departed from the port. At 9:00 AM, the ship was near a hidden reef next to Xiaozhui Mountain at the mouth of Quanzhou (marked on the nautical chart as being six feet above low tide). The ship's owner, Japanese national Teiichi Kotani, was on duty. The Japanese national was not familiar with the route and mistakenly steered into the reef, causing it to run aground. The bottom of the ship was severely damaged by the reef.

Ship Damage: The bottom of the ship, from the first cabin to the second cabin, was breached for over 100 feet, with eight iron plates and dozens of transverse ribs damaged. Fortunately, the bottom of the ship was double-layered, preventing it from sinking. However, the loss is estimated to be at least 30,000 yuan. Later, at high tide, it managed to reverse out of danger and ventured to Shanghai for repairs.

Damaged an American Warship: Yesterday, the ship arrived at the Jiangnan Shipyard at the entrance of Shanghai for repairs. Unexpectedly, when entering the dock, it veered and collided with an American warship parked on the riverside, causing significant damage to the warship's hull. Yesterday, the captain of the warship reported to the harbor master. After verifying the extent of the damage, a negotiation will be initiated, and Dalian will be asked for compensation.

Issue of Arms Found on a Shipping Vessel

Headquarters Ordered That Those Unrelated to the Ship Not Be Detained

The Shanghai Shipping Association previously reported that troops stationed along the Yangtze River would often detain ships without permission on the pretext of searching passengers for concealed weapons, preventing them from sailing. Although the shipping bureaus in various places negotiated on reasonable grounds, they rarely succeeded, hindering transportation significantly. Therefore, a special report was submitted to the Ministry, asking it to instruct troops stationed in various places that, if weapons were found on ships, ships should not be detained without permission unless the ship's crew was involved, in order to maintain the shipping industry. It is now learned that the Shipping Association received instructions from the Ministry yesterday, stating: "The report regarding the troops stationed along the river not being allowed to detain shipping vessels without permission has been noted. In addition to the Ministry sending a general letter to the troops stationed along the river to inform them of this matter, General Commander Chiang has also approved an order instructing the troops stationed along the river that, in the future, if passengers are found to have concealed weapons on ships, ships should not be detained if the ship is not involved, in order to maintain the shipping industry. You are hereby informed of this order."

Crisis in the Future of China's Egg Industry

American Fresh Eggs Are Being Imported

China has always been known for its agricultural products. However, in recent years, the government has paid too little attention to research and improvement, and it has been declining. The increasing population and quantity of rice and wheat, and the declining foreign trade in silk and tea, are all significant indicators. Fresh eggs have also been a major export of our country. Recently, a surprising message was received that a major company in Hong Kong imported 100 dozen good fresh eggs from the United States in August of this year. Each dozen was sold for HK$1.60, and the goods were sold out within one day of arrival. 1,000 dozen were purchased and sold out. In the future, they will continue to order from the United States. Although there are a few new-style chicken farms in Shanghai, they are all too small in scope to meet this major request. This alone shows the urgent need for agricultural improvement. The improvement must not only be in quantity, but also in quality. In this time of national crisis and the promotion of national goods, this kind of news deserves serious attention from the government and society. We must act quickly.

Letter from the Harbor Quarantine Office to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Regarding the Inland River Shipping Industry's Opposition to Ship Double Disinfection

The Harbor Quarantine Office has replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce in response to some misunderstandings regarding the inner harbor shipping industry's ship disinfection, stating: "Regarding your letter No. 208 dated the 11th of this month, stating that the National Harbor Quarantine Office is forcibly charging fees, which is unprecedented, and that the voyage is very short, making disinfection unnecessary, and requesting that the Chamber forward this to the Social Bureau to stop it, and stating that the Shanghai Inland River Shipping Industry Association member, Xiexing Shipping Bureau, reported that the Quarantine Office has been forcing them to pay fees in recent days, etc., the Chamber has sent a cable to the Ministry and requested free processing. This office is responsible for quarantine, directly responsible for the health of the people in the port, and indirectly responsible for international health missions. We have repeatedly explained this and sent notices and quarantine and disinfection regulations for you to forward. However, the Inland River Shipping Industry Association considers the execution of official duties to be forced charging, and considers the important administration related to international health to be unprecedented. This is an undeniable misidentification. As for the claim that the voyage is very short and that there have never been epidemics, making disinfection and prevention unnecessary, if an epidemic were to break out, it would be too late to remedy it. The current situation in provinces such as Shanxi and Shaanxi can serve as a warning. As for the request to forward this to the Social Bureau to stop it, it shows a lack of understanding of the organization of administrative organs. It is no wonder that there is a misidentification and a lack of understanding of the facts. Furthermore, the Xiexing Shipping Bureau and other companies in the same industry, such as Lixing, Gongmao, etc., have already signed contracts for ship disinfection. Therefore, resisting health administration and disregarding human morality is one matter, and violating the contract is another matter. The Inner Harbor Ship Double Disinfection Regulations were promulgated and implemented on July 27 of this year. Later, because the regulations were not exhaustive, they were approved for modification and re-promulgated on September 20. The fee for ship disinfection cannot be compared to national or local taxes. This office needs to use a lot of medicines for ship fumigation and disinfection. The minor public fee paid once every six months by shipowners for the right to disinfection and hygiene is also a reasonable obligation that they should fulfill. The funds allocated by the Customs Office are the operating expenses allocated to this office by the state. The request for free disinfection is like asking a clever woman to cook without rice. In addition to awaiting instructions from the Ministry, Article 6 of the Inner Harbor Ship Double Disinfection Regulations states that 'this Quarantine Office may provide free medical consultation to shipowners in the port who have minor illnesses or injuries. In addition, this office has a well-equipped epidemic prevention hospital. If any epidemic victims are discovered, they may be sent to the hospital for diagnosis and treatment.' This office is not just collecting fees without doing practical things. We are afraid that the outside world does not understand, so we are including this information. We hope that your association will assist in national administration, and that you will carefully explain and guide the preparations of the masses. This will be very beneficial to the future of humanity and hygiene. The reason for the letter is as above. Please review it. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, November 18."

The Victim Bravely Catches a Thief

The Thief Fired Three Shots, None Hit

Ling Jilin, a local carpenter, residing at No. 1350, Fugangli, Avenue Edward VII, had six thieves break into his house at around 6 p.m. last night. Two of them were armed with handguns. At Gordon Road, one thief was apprehended. Seeing this, the other thieves fired a shot, but fortunately, the bullet did not hit. As a result, one thief was still apprehended and taken to the authorities.

Wang Yifei Angered by Japan, Attempts Suicide by Jumping into the Huangpu River and Is Rescued

At around 10 p.m. the night before last, a young man at the Tenth Wharf outside Maojia Lane, Dadongmen, Nanshi, jumped into the Huangpu River unnoticed, attempting suicide. Hu Yucheng, a guard at the first post, spotted him and rushed to call for help from nearby boatmen. They managed to rescue the young man. He was taken to the first district's general office across the river for preliminary questioning. He stated that his name was Wang Yifei, 18 years old, from Ningbo. He had been working as a small accountant in a Japanese household in Qingdao. After the outrageous Japanese occupied our country's eastern provinces, the news spread, and because I am also a citizen of the Republic of China, I should naturally fulfill my responsibilities as a citizen. Therefore, I resigned from my job. After leaving, I took a ship to Shanghai to look for old friends and find a new place to live. Unexpectedly, my fate was unfortunate. After many days of searching, I could not find a place to settle down. In addition, I learned from the newspapers every day that the hateful and barbaric Japanese were invading our country more and more. Therefore, I was extremely frustrated. I thought that living in this turbid world was meaningless. That is why I came here today to commit suicide by jumping into the Huangpu River, in order to end my miserable life and hopefully awaken my countrymen to rise up and resist Japan. It was ordered that a document be prepared and sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for placement.

Case of Watchman-Police Beating a Rickshaw Puller

Released on a Fifty Yuan Good Behavior Bond

The Great American Evening Post reports that two men, Sa Huaxin and Meng Geerxin, watchman-police employed by the New Kang Land Company, were accused of beating a rickshaw puller on Central Road last Tuesday. After several days of trial in the British Police Court, a verdict was reached this morning. The verdict made an important statement regarding the status of watchman-police, declaring that neither the regulations of the Foreign Concessions nor the police regulations of the Municipal Council stipulate that watchman-police employed by private entities possess greater authority than ordinary private citizens. Therefore, Sa Huaxin was found guilty of ordinary battery and was released on a fifty-yuan good behavior bond. Meng Geerxin was acquitted leniently due to insufficient evidence.

Great Alliance for Abstaining from Cigarettes

Mr. Wang Longchao, the initiator of the Juvenile Propaganda Group in the Small West Gate of this city, recognizing that the harm caused by cigarettes far exceeds that of opium, has organized the "Great Alliance for Abstaining from Cigarettes." Those who do not smoke pledge to abstain for life, and those who do smoke quit immediately, saving this unnecessary expense and donating it to the national salvation fund. Since its establishment, hundreds of people have registered. It is recently reported that the organization has manufactured silver chicken-heart badges to be issued to members to wear and demonstrate their determination.

French Company Delivers New-Style Trolleys

For the comfort of passengers, the French Trolley Company has ordered ten of the latest model trolleys and trailers each from a famous factory in France, which have been shipped to Shanghai from France. These vehicles are luxuriously equipped, and the trailers resemble the trolleys, except that they do not have engine compartments. The electric lights used are also twice as bright as those in the old cars, resulting in ample lighting. Currently, five cars have been assembled in Shanghai, and others are being rushed to completion. Yesterday, several trolleys from Xujiahui to the Sixteen Pups were put into service, and passengers all praised them for being smoother and more comfortable than the old cars.

Measurement Inspection Started in Four Districts of Songwan, Zhabei, and Pudong Yesterday

Since the implementation of the new system of weights and measures in this city, the districts in the Nanshi area have been inspected one by one and are now using the new system. The four districts of Wusong, Jiangwan, Zhabei, and Pudong also began inspections yesterday. Three inspectors from the Weights and Measures Verification Institute, together with three police chiefs from the Public Security Bureau, are conducting door-to-door inspections until completed.

Murdered Male Body on Zhongshan Road

Behind the Central Mint on Zhongshan Road in Zhabei, at around 5:30 PM yesterday, a man was assassinated and fell dead on the ground. The deceased was about four feet tall, with a round head and long face. He had gunshot wounds to his left chest and left side of his head. He was wearing a black wool camel hair robe, blue thread cotton trousers, a white silk short shirt, and black satin shoes. He appeared to be about twenty-eight or twenty-nine years old. Upon receiving the news, the Public Security Bureau of the Fourth District immediately dispatched police to investigate and apprehend the murderer. A letter was found near the deceased, addressed to Yao Jintang, which may be the name of the deceased. The district has requested the court to conduct an autopsy today.

Violin Master Jascha Heifetz Arrives in Shanghai

The world-renowned violin master Jascha Heifetz is the only master violinist of modern times. He has been famous for more than ten years and has performed in major cities in Europe and America, where he has been very well received. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday for his third world tour of performances and is staying at the Hua Mao Hotel on the Bund. He will perform three times at the New Light Theater on Ningbo Road. The first performance is scheduled for tomorrow night (the 20th). He is accompanied by his wife, Florence Vidor, who is a famous movie star.

Shanghai Bank's Zhonghongqiao Branch Opens Tomorrow

For the convenience of people in this city, the Shanghai Commercial and Savings Bank has successively added branches in Hongkou, Jing'an Temple, Avenue Joffre, Baxianqiao, Xiaodongmen, West Gate, Jielu, and Tilanqiao. Now, in view of the numerous factories and dense population in the Zhonghongqiao area, a branch has been established at No. 73 Dongxi Huade Road, which will open for business tomorrow (the 20th).

Xu Lingyun Sues to Be Relieved of Responsibility for Guaranteeing Loans

Ai Jianming States He Should Bear Joint Responsibility

Xu Lingyun, a prominent silk merchant in this city, organized the Yifengxiang Silk Firm in 1929, located on Taiwan Road (inside Xu's residence). Xu held three shares, Huang Jinchen held three shares, Ai Jianming held three shares, and a Mr. Chen held one share. At that time, Ai Jianming was elected as manager, and Xu Lingyun and Huang Jinchen were the resident shareholder representatives, so that the assistant manager could consult with them on matters nearby. Last year, shareholder representative Huang Jinchen handled the silk factory's mortgage loan, amounting to over 700,000 yuan from Dingyuan. Later, because the price of silk fell daily, Huang Jinchen died this spring. At the end of last year, the amount of money exchanged with various banks was as high as 400,000 to 500,000 yuan. In order to maintain credit, the firm had Xu Lingyun and Ai Jianming jointly guarantee the loan and repeatedly extend the term. When the term was about to expire at the end of October this year, Xu Lingyun was afraid that the banks would press for payment and he would have no excuse to give, so he sued Ai Jianming in the Shanghai District Court at the beginning of last month, demanding to be relieved of the guarantee responsibility, on the grounds that Ai Jianming induced him to act as guarantor (because Ai Jianming lives in the Chinese district). Yesterday, the court summoned the defendant, Ai Jianming, who did not appear, and appointed lawyer Chen Wenzhao to appear on his behalf, stating that the defendant and the plaintiff have the same shares in the case, and the guarantee responsibility is also the same. The powers of the manager and the shareholder's resident representative, as well as the horse fees, etc., are all the same. Moreover, the silk factory's mortgage loan was handled by Huang Jinchen. The plaintiff lives in the firm day and night, so how could he not know about the exchange of money with the banks, etc. After debating with the plaintiff's lawyer, he stated to the court that the plaintiff, Xu Lingyun, had recently filed a criminal breach of trust lawsuit in the First Special District Court. The same facts should not be accused in different ways. If a criminal offense occurs, it can be reported in the civil court, etc. Judge Fan of the trial ordered that the hearing be adjourned and that witnesses be summoned again and other shareholders be notified to participate.

Over Two Hundred Gold Yuan Stolen from a Brothel

Ninth Sister, Lao Jiu, Feared Being Punished

Although Did Not Steal, Willing to Compensate

Result: Fine of Thirty Yuan

Cheng Jiudi, the owner of the brothel at No. 700 Small Garden, Zhejiang Road, whose original name is Cheng Jiudi, discovered on the 14th of this month that more than two hundred silver dollars placed in the kitchen had disappeared. Later, a tin box containing banknotes was found under the sofa in the room. Upon opening it, it was empty. He then reported it to the Lao Zha Police Station, who ordered detective Zhu Shanghe to conduct a review. It was learned that the stolen banknotes were undoubtedly stolen by someone inside, because Cheng Jiudi placed the banknotes very secretly, and outsiders would not know. The people in the brothel were summoned to the police station for questioning one by one. At that time, the prostitute Ninth Sister, Lao Jiu (original name Qian Suzhen, from Pudong, 19 years old) suddenly claimed that although she did not steal the money, she was willing to compensate the full amount. Suspecting her suspicious behavior, she was immediately detained. Yesterday morning, she was escorted to the Simple Court of the First Special Court. Police Lawyer Qian Xunjiu prosecuted her for theft under Article 337 of the Criminal Code. Then, Cheng Jiudi submitted a petition stating the previous situation, and claimed that many people enter and exit his room, so it is impossible to determine whether the money was stolen by Qian Suzhen, but her usual behavior is quite good, etc. When questioned, Qian Suzhen said that she did not actually steal the money. When she was at the police station, she said that she was willing to compensate because she was afraid of being beaten by the foreign detectives, and asked for understanding. She also retained lawyer Jiang Baoli to defend her. Judge Jiang Gongliang reviewed the confession and sentenced Qian Zhen to a fine of thirty yuan in court.

Lawsuit for Check Not Being Paid in Cash

When the Zhihe Yongji Bank closed down, it issued a large number of high-value checks. The payees, unable to cash them, filed lawsuits one after another. Madie, the manager of the British firm Wanlai Foreign Firm, also received a check from the bank for 50,000 taels of silver. The origin of the check was the payment from Shen Chengfu, a comprador of the Taihe Foreign Firm, for Madie's purchase of cotton, due on August 28. However, on August 19, the Zhihe Bank closed down. Madie claimed that Shen Yingxiang, the father of Shen Chengfu, was the manager of the Zhihe Bank, which was clearly a conspiracy to defraud property. He then retained lawyer Wu Linkun to file a criminal self-prosecution against Shen Yingxiang and Shen Chengfu, father and son, in the First Special Court. However, Shen Chengfu had already fled without a trace. Yesterday afternoon, when the court summoned Shen Yingxiang for trial, he claimed that he had been in contact with Taihe Foreign Firm. Shen Chengfu used to issue checks, and he would always deliver the silver on time. At the beginning of August, he issued a large number of checks, but he did not deliver the silver, causing Zhihe to have insufficient funds and be forced to close down. There was no collusion. Lawyer Wu then requested an investigation of the accounts. Judge Jiang then ordered that the case be adjourned for further hearing. Shen Yingxiang was required to provide a shopkeeper's guarantee that he would be available when summoned.

Zheng Hongyao Flees After Deceiving Goods

Creditors' Group Has Filed a Lawsuit According to Law

Zheng Honghui, the owner and manager of Zheng Yiji Chaozhou Office in Shanghai on Taiwan Road in the French Concession, under the pretext of procuring goods, defrauded more than 20 fruit wholesalers in Nanshi Sixteen Pups of fruit worth over 10,000 gold yuan. He also used the same trick to defraud a huge amount of goods from various candy, groceries, and foreign goods shops, all paid with post-dated bad checks from a certain bank. Before the checks were due, Zheng took his family and fled without a trace, leaving only goods that had not been shipped out in the shop (namely small fruit candies), worth about 20 gold yuan. When the check holders went to cash the checks upon maturity, they learned that the owner had gone bankrupt and fled. They immediately formed a creditors' group and hired lawyer Zhou Xiao'an. Yesterday, they gathered all the creditors to discuss how to recover the debts. The candy and grocery creditors had already joined. Yesterday, they first filed a request with the Second District Court of the Special District for a provisional attachment order to be executed quickly, so as to avoid the remaining goods being delayed and rotting, and to protect the capital of the creditors.

Refugees Freeze to Death in the Alley

In an alley on Linping Road in Hongzhen, north of Shanghai, there are Jiangbei refugees living in the open. As the weather gets colder, they lack clothing and food, and many are freezing and starving and becoming ill. Yesterday, a refugee died in the alley. He was about fifty years old and was still wearing a tattered blue cloth short shirt and trousers. He was as thin as a stick. After being informed, the Fourth Division of the Fifth District ordered the local bailiff to report it to the District Court for an inquest. Prosecutor Wang and others arrived at the scene and confirmed that the death was due to illness. The body was taken to the mortuary.

Man Crushed to Death by Songhu Railway Train

The Songhu Railway train, when traveling to the Nanhe Station Miaohou Bridge in Zhanghuabang, Wusong, the afternoon before yesterday, a man was walking on the tracks. He was knocked down by the train's footboard and run over, immediately losing his life. The Railway Police Department ordered the local bailiff to report it to the District Court for an inquest yesterday. Prosecutor Wang and others arrived at the scene and found that the deceased was about twenty years old, wearing a blue cloth short shirt and trousers. The injured parts were the forehead and waist. It was determined that the death was caused by injuries. The body was ordered to be taken to the mortuary, awaiting relatives to claim it.

The Ferocity of the Murderous Thugs

Claimed to Be From Little Ningbo Before Leaving

The Mediator Was Slapped in the Face

Wang Aqiao, also known as Weng Ajiao, a 22-year-old from Ningbo who worked as a cargo caller, recently became acquainted with Zhang Laoqi, a former prostitute from Suzhou. Zhang had a smoking addiction. The night before last, Wang and his uncle accompanied Zhang to Yan Boying's Suzhou-style room at No. 10 Yuqing Lane, Xixinqiao Street, French Concession, to indulge. At 8:45 PM, more than ten enemies suddenly rushed in, each wielding sharp weapons. A man wearing a black serge gown and a copper basin hat, speaking in the local dialect, led the group. The rest were dressed in blue cloth short coats and long clothes. The leader entered the room and called out for Ajiao. Wang, who was lying on the opium bed, thought it was a friend and got up to greet him. The leader pointed a pistol at Wang and ordered him to take off his coat. As soon as Wang took off his coat, the leader's accomplices took out sharp axes and hacked at Wang's shoulders, back, hands, and feet, inflicting more than ten axe wounds. Wang fell to the ground. While the attack was taking place, the assailants guarded the stairs and the door, preventing anyone from entering or leaving. They said to the bystanders, "Go away, this is none of your business." Yan Boying pleaded with the thugs, but was slapped in the face. The assailants, seeing that their goal had been achieved, fled in a chaotic rush. Before leaving, they shouted loudly, "I am from Little Ningbo, see where I am!" After the assailants left, Wang's uncle and concubine hired a car to take Wang to Renji Hospital for treatment. Yan Boying reported the incident to the police station, which sent detectives to investigate the scene and arrest the murderers. However, Wang died in the hospital at 4:45 AM yesterday due to his severe injuries. Wang's uncle and concubine had already left the hospital, so the hospital notified the police station, which sent detectives to transport the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Sub-Hall, the morgue. Because the body could not be identified, the Second Special Court was notified. Prosecutor Ding Shikui, along with forensic doctors Wei Ligong and Jiang Qu, and clerk Peng Xu, arrived at the scene at 10:00 AM. After examining the body, they sat at the public table. The patrol reported the previous situation, and witness Yan Boying testified about the circumstances of the deceased being hacked. Mr. Ding announced that the deceased Wang Aqiao had died from axe wounds inflicted during his life. If the deceased's relatives come to claim the body for burial, they will be allowed to do so; otherwise, the Tongren Fuyuan Hall will arrange for the burial. After the examination, at 11:00 AM, the deceased's concubine, Zhang Laoqi, finally found the deceased's mother, Weng Zhang, and brought her to the hall to sign a guarantee to claim the body for burial.

Yan Jinbiao Disagrees With Death Sentence

Appeal Case Scheduled for Pronouncement

Yan Jinbiao, also known as Yan Er, from Funing, Jiangbei, previously organized a gang to commit three robberies in the French Concession and opened fire in the Fashang Hotel, killing three people. Afterwards, he was arrested by the French police and sent to the Second Special Court. After the trial, Yan was found guilty of robbery and murder and sentenced to death. Because Yan did not agree with the initial trial, he hired a lawyer and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the High Court. Yesterday morning, Judge Guo Dezhang, along with Associate Judges Zhang Chaozuo and Li Changnian, and Chief Prosecutor Peng Wangxin, sat in the Second Criminal Court to question him. Yan Jinbiao stated that he was 31 years old and from Funing. When asked if he had committed any crimes before, he replied that he had been framed and sentenced to nine months in prison in the British Concession court in February 1929. When asked if he was also known as Yan Jinbiao, he replied that he had changed his name to Yan Dongbo. When asked if he had committed three robberies with the fugitive Shi Renwen and others, and committed murder with Yang Jiucheng, Li Guoren and others in the hotel, he replied that he was really wronged. He had been a military messenger in Xuzhou in 1928 and came to Shanghai in 1929. He was arrested in the British Concession, and he dared not steal, let alone commit murder. When asked why he confessed everything in the first trial, he replied that he had been coerced into confessing in the police station in the first trial. When asked if he admitted to participating in the robbery in the first trial and if stolen goods and two pawn tickets from the victim's house were found at his place and identified by the victim, he replied that his brother-in-law, Feng Damin, and his wife Zhang's lover were both robbers, and the pawn tickets belonged to Feng Da and were not obtained by him through robbery. When asked if he confessed in the first trial that he, Li Guoren, and Yang Jiucheng conspired to rob a pawnshop on Chongqing Road in the Chunjiang Hotel, fearing that Jiang Zhonghan, Xia Rongsheng, and a Mr. Xue would report them, so they first shot them to death and then went to rob the pawnshop, and that after the agreement, they went to the Fashang Hotel, where he fired three shots first and the rest were fired by Li and others, he replied that Li Guoren said to Yang Jiucheng while eating at his concubine's house in August that his brother had been murdered and that he wanted to call Yang Jiucheng and him to take revenge, but he did not go. At this point, Chief Prosecutor Peng stood up to make his arguments, stating that the appellant Yan Jinbiao's three counts of breaking into people's houses to rob and committing murder had been thoroughly investigated in the first trial, and there were records to prove it. Now the appellant has suddenly recanted his confession, but has not presented any concrete evidence to the contrary, and his statements are all empty words and difficult to believe. He asked for a judgment according to the law. Police lawyer Gu Shouxi said that the appellant was questioned several times in the first trial and had always admitted his guilt. His lawyer believed that the judgment of the first trial was very legal and requested that the appeal be dismissed and the original judgment be upheld. After the appellant's lawyer made his defense, Judge Guo announced the end of the debate and said that the judgment would be announced on a scheduled date.

Construction Worker Falls to Death From High Building

Gu Gentao, a 21-year-old from Pudong who worked as a plasterer and lived at No. 10 Jungong Road, was working on the second floor of a newly built ten-story building opposite the Municipal Council on Simalu at around 4:15 PM yesterday. He accidentally lost his footing and fell, suffering a severe head injury and barely breathing. The supervisor of the construction site sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment by car, but it was ineffective. He died a quarter of an hour later. The body was transferred to the morgue by the hospital to await the court's examination.

Old Woman Violently Hacked With Six Axes

Deng Zheng Died on the Spot

Lin Yuan Reported and is a Suspect

Deng Zheng, an elderly woman of 76 years of age, a Cantonese, residing at No. 13, Lane 29, Jiangbian Road, Gaochang Temple, South Shanghai, had one son and four daughters. Her son, Zheng Zhuoen, was 35 years old and had three sons. The eldest son, Zhi Di, was eight years old and lived with his grandmother, Deng Zheng, at Gaochang Temple. Zheng Zhuoen used to work as a carpenter at the Jiangnan Shipyard but had quit and now worked as a carpenter at the Wanneng Machine Factory at No. 164 Baotong Road, Hongkou. Due to inconvenient transportation, he lived separately from his mother, Deng Zheng. Unexpectedly, at around 8:00 AM yesterday, Deng Zheng was assassinated at home by someone who broke in and hacked the old woman's head six times with an axe. One axe wound below her ear and on her neck was fatal, causing her to fall to the ground and die instantly. Afterwards, Lin Yuan, a 29-year-old Cantonese who lives at No. 24, Lane 41, Jiangbian Road, Gaochang Temple, who makes a living as a tailor and is now a gambler, reported to the police officer on duty that Deng Zheng had been hacked to death. The police officer on duty brought the reporter to the Gaochang Temple Police Station in the Second District for custody. At the same time, police were sent to investigate the deceased's home. According to the deceased's eldest grandson, Zhi Di, Lin Yuan was the perpetrator. The fourth daughter of the woman also said that a few days ago, Lin Yuan came with an axe, pretending to borrow an awl, but did not dare to act because there were many people present. The police station, suspecting Lin Yuan, detained him and sent him to the Second District Headquarters, while reporting to the District Court. At 3:00 PM, the court sent a prosecutor to conduct an autopsy, confirming that she had been assassinated and had six axe wounds to the head, with one to the neck being fatal. A coroner's report was filled out, and the family was ordered to prepare a coffin for burial. The suspected perpetrator, Lin Yuan, who was sent by the Second District, will be thoroughly investigated upon his arrival.

Jin Fusheng Lightly Punished for Misappropriating Funds Due to Honesty in the Past

Fine of One Hundred Yuan

Jin Fusheng, a local, had been working as an accountant at the Continental and Liwei Automobile Company at No. 694 Jing'an Temple Road for four years. Recently, the company's manager, a foreigner named Ma Xu, discovered that Jin had privately collected 1,011.5 yuan in account fees and 280.65 taels of silver from the Office of the Financial Advisor of the Ministry of Finance between March and July of this year and had used them privately. He reported it to the Xinzha Police Station the day before yesterday, and Chinese detective Shao Jingfan and foreign detective Yi Wenen were dispatched to arrest Jin and bring him to the police station. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang presented the facts of the case, and the company's representative, a foreigner, complained about the defendant's private collection of account fees, but because the defendant had been employed for four years and was usually very honest, he requested a lenient sentence. When questioned, the defendant admitted to the charges. Judge Wu Tingqi reviewed the confession and sentenced Jin Fusheng to a fine of one hundred yuan for a crime of handling affairs for others, intending to obtain illegal benefits for himself and violating his duties, causing damage to the property of the principal. If the fine is commuted to imprisonment, it will be calculated at three yuan per day.

Jiaoji Railway National Coal Freight Surcharge Postponed

Extension of Three Months From November 1

The case of the Jiaoji Railway increasing national coal freight rates has caused a reaction from all levels of the country. Yesterday, the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce received instructions from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, instructing the governor to investigate the case of the Jiaoji Railway's increase in national coal freight rates. After the Ministry reported on the handling of the case, the railway authorities sent letters stating that they had agreed with the representatives of various coal merchants to temporarily suspend the method of increasing coal freight rates on various roads. All increased coal freight rates per catty since May 1 of this year will be temporarily suspended for three months from November 1. This order is for your information.

Pushan Hospital Has Excellent Performance

Pushan Villa, which is separated by the Pushan Obstetrics Hospital in Zhabei, also conducts daily medical treatment and medicine distribution, which has been a benefit for many years, benefiting the poor and sick. Recently, with the rising cost of living, the poor and sick are unable to afford medical treatment and go to the hospital for treatment. From January to October of this year, a total of more than 42,000 medical treatments and medicine distributions were conducted. The director of the hospital, Mr. Shi Yixuan, has scientific equipment and medicine, and the layout is well organized. Every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday, Mr. Xu Deliang and others are invited to teach English and various nursing courses to nurses free of charge, in order to train specialized talents who will benefit society in the future. However, the hospital is entirely a charity, and the annual expenses depend entirely on donations from philanthropists from all walks of life, which is very stretched. It is hoped that kind-hearted gentlemen will enthusiastically donate to help, so that the hospital's good deeds can be maintained.

Housing Dispute at Daoda Baoshu Two Lanes, Aiwunyi Road

Residents and shopkeepers of Daoda Baoshu Two Lanes on Aiwunyi Road received notices from the landlord to renovate and were required to move out before January 10th. The residents and shopkeepers felt that at this time of national crisis, with the situation serious, all industries depressed, and society uneasy, the landlord's action was not only disregarding the overall situation but also coming right before the New Year, which would certainly cause great losses and was difficult to bear. Yesterday, all the tenants held a meeting and decided to send several representatives to the landlord's place this afternoon to express their views.

Publication of "Outline of Japanese Economic Power in the Three Eastern Provinces"

Since the Mukden Incident, the Industry and Commerce Inquiry Bureau of the Ministry of Industry has been collecting materials on various aspects of Japanese economic power in the Three Eastern Provinces. In addition to publishing them in the bureau's "China English Economic Monthly" and "Industry and Commerce Bi-monthly," a small booklet, "Outline of Japanese Economic Power in the Three Eastern Provinces," has been specially compiled for the convenience of general readers. The content includes railways, finance, agriculture, forestry, industry, and commerce operated by Japan in our Northeast, as well as various joint ventures and a general overview of the journey, which is extremely detailed. The book has now been published. For the sake of popularization, each issue only costs one dime for printing. Major bookstores in this city, such as the Commercial Press and Liming Bookstore, are selling it.

Consultation Hours of National Doctor Zhuang Shijun

Since passing the first registration examination of the Municipal Health Bureau, the national doctor Zhuang Shijun has only been able to accept invitations for consultations from relatives and friends in his spare time due to other duties. However, those who have been treated by him have all been cured with medicine. Seeing that the number of patients seeking treatment has been increasing recently, and that the lack of fixed consultation hours has caused patients to travel back and forth in vain, Dr. Zhuang has decided to set his consultation hours from 5:00 PM to 7:00 PM for outpatient visits and 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM for house calls, starting from today. No appointments will be made after these hours, and the consultation fee is at the patient's discretion. Poor patients can be sent for consultation. The clinic is located at 357 Weihaiwei Road.

News from the Municipal Joint District Branches

Seventeenth District: The Seventeenth District Branch of the Special District Citizens' Federation yesterday issued a solicitation for contributions to reward Chairman Ma's isolated army in Heilongjiang for resisting Japan, stating: "For the past twenty years in our country, the army that punishes the people and executes the crimes has been seen many times, and the articles denouncing and reforming the government have been commonplace. Upon examination of the reasons for this, it is found that brothers are fighting each other, and family members are killing each other. You rise up and I fall, using violence to replace violence, only creating a scene of wailing everywhere and people living in poverty, which has been the case for more than a day. Now, the violent Japanese have invaded and forcibly occupied the three provinces. The officials in power, on the other hand, are silent and unknown. They do not resist when the soldiers are under the city, and they do not ask when the blood is dyed on the necks of the people. Where is the majesty of punishing crimes and denouncing them in the past? The only one who can consider the crying of Qin Ting and ask for help for the people is Chairman Ma Zhanshan of Heilongjiang Province alone. It is heard that Lord Ma's isolated army is fighting bravely against the savage soldiers in Heilongjiang, fighting thousands of miles, vowing to die to wash away the humiliation. All of our compatriots should spare no effort to reward the saviors who are fighting for national glory and loving the country, which is also a way to follow the ancient people's virtue of offering food and drink. Therefore, this branch has resolved to carry out reward work through regular meetings, and has requested the Bank of China in this district to directly remit money to Heilongjiang Province, without charging remittance fees, to show its enthusiasm. Moreover, Comrade Hua Xin Timber Industry of this association was the first to donate two hundred foreign dollars for remittance. The patriotic enthusiasm of your office has long been well-known. We hope that you will actively donate, send it directly to the Bank of China, remit it immediately after delivery, and there will be receipts from the bank as proof. Please do not take it lightly. This is the announcement of the Seventeenth District Branch of the Special District Citizens' Federation of Shanghai."

Letter to the Editor

What is a Practical and Effective Way to Boycott Japanese Goods?

— Zheng Hongsheng

Relying solely on a few people to shout and run around to boycott Japanese goods cannot popularize it everywhere, nor can it be permanently effective. To seek practical and universal methods, there must be a permanent organization that works to promote and research in the consumer markets everywhere, so that the general public will voluntarily not buy enemy goods. Over time, enemy goods will disappear from our market. The following plan is proposed: (1) Chambers of Commerce in various parts of the country should establish commodity research institutes (where there are no chambers of commerce, they can also be established by relevant agencies). The tasks are roughly as follows: (1) Identify the country of origin of commodities (2) Study the quality of commodities (3) Investigate the sales channels of commodities (4) Study the methods of replacing commodities with domestic goods (5) Introduce domestic goods. It is best for the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to take the lead in initiating the above-mentioned research institute, formulating regulations, and sending circulars to chambers of commerce in various places to establish them uniformly. (2) Conduct a commodity survey. After the research institute is established, it will immediately conduct a commodity survey. In order to achieve the purpose of the task, an example of the survey form is as follows:

Commodity Name Brand Manufacturer Identification Method Advantages and Disadvantages Price Sales Remarks

Monosodium glutamate Fo Shou China Tianchu Monosodium Glutamate Factory There is a word invented by Wu Yun Chu The taste is fresh, clean, pure, and vegetarian Medium-sized bottle, 48 cents

Ajinomoto Japan Suzuki Store Both bottled and canned have oriental characters The same purpose, the price is more expensive due to the gold exchange rate

Matches Phoenix Sweden Not damp Copper four pieces

Matches Beauty China Greater China Company More stems, more durable Copper three pieces

The above table is filled in based on what I remember. In addition, such as the camel hair velour made by Jintian Xiang Textile Factory recently, and the invention of the National Goods Raw Material Research Association, which has the same sauce color as Japanese goods, can all be used as research materials for promoting domestic goods. If the Chambers of Commerce in Tianjin, Guangdong, Shanghai, and Wuhan conduct a clear investigation by category first and issue it to various places for reference, then various places only need to fill in the forms in the same way or selectively re-check them once and post them on the doors of various stores for people to view. (3) Commodity labels. All stores that display various commodities must mark the country of origin with labels. This label can be made by the research institute based on the quality of the commodities, charged at cost, and distributed for application. With such a clear investigation, stores will not dare to openly sell enemy goods, nor will they dare to muddle through and pass off enemy goods as domestic goods or goods from other countries. The general public will also be aware of the quality of the goods, whether there are domestic goods to replace them, and know what to choose when buying. The matter is easy to do and the effect is sure to be great. In addition, publicizing and lecturing to the civilian teams at any time will also help the progress of this matter.

Reply from Good-Hearted Zi Jun (Omitted)

(Reply) Your letter discusses "At this time when the violent Japanese are rampant and the situation is urgent, enemy goods should not be allowed to be sold hastily." This is a very insightful point of view. Please also refer to the article "It's Not Difficult to Boycott Japanese Goods" by Mr. Xia, which was specially published in the fourth edition of the Shen Bao on November 16, 17, 18, and 19. It discusses the matter in great detail and can be used as a reference for you. Respectfully reply.

Letters

Dear Editor, I read a news item in today's newspaper about the strike of the employees of the Datong Bookstore, and it was said that a precondition has been put forward, etc. This does not match the facts. Our association has not put forward a precondition. The so-called precondition in your newspaper is the condition of the final concession requested by the trade union office and the company before the strike. However, the company still could not understand at that time and had no sincerity to accept it, which aroused the public anger of all the employees and led to a strike by all of them. The strikers this time include all the workers in the printing press, letterpress department, color printing department, type casting department, Chinese and Western typesetting department, photogravure department, valuable securities letterpress department, copper mold department, etc. The officials who have joined the association in the General Affairs Department, Publishing Department, Promotion Department, Branch Office Affairs Department, Accounting Department, Warehouse Department, Proofreading Department, and Editorial Department are currently working in the company only a small part of the officials who have not joined the association. I would like to ask you to correct this. Sincerely, Datong Bookstore Branch Office of the Publishing Industry Trade Union, November 18.

Dear Editor, I read a news item in your newspaper's local news section on the 13th about the private establishment of a poem riddle gambling platform in Minhang Min Garden. This does not match the facts. This garden has been established as a public entertainment venue for more than ten years. Whether it performs obscene flower drum opera is self-evident. The poem riddles are a matter of literary elegance. It is a matter of reputation and should be communicated to request your newspaper to make corrections in order to show the facts. With great gratitude, Minhang Min Garden, November 18.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday said that it was cloudy and cold on the coast here and in the Yangtze River Basin. There was snow on the Shandong coast. There was a strong seasonal wind from the northwest to the northeast along the four coastal areas. The weather between Kyushu and the Ogasawara Islands was bad due to a hurricane passing through and moving northeast. Its center moved to within 120 miles of the intersection of 27 degrees north latitude and 237 degrees east longitude at noon. Another hurricane in the Pacific Ocean moved to within 120 miles of the intersection of 13 degrees north latitude and 140 degrees east longitude at noon and moved northwest. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 58.8 degrees and the lowest was 51.4 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 68.4 degrees and the lowest was 45.3 degrees.
