Free Talk

Memoirs of Dailiang

— Yanzi

The Treaty of Shimonoseki was concluded, and Taiwan was ceded. Public opinion generally blamed Li Hongzhang, the minister who negotiated the peace. In fact, Japan originally intended to acquire the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang. Li insisted on not agreeing, so those who ceded Taiwan had to think of the next best thing. At that time, the Japanese people all blamed Ito Hirobumi for not getting the eastern provinces, and some even threatened to see him with knives. When the treaty was signed, Li knew that there would be resistance among the Taiwanese, so he sent his son Jingfang to hand over the territory. The Taiwanese people protested loudly and elected Governor Tang Jingsong as President, and Liu Yongfu as commander-in-chief, and raised troops to resist. The Japanese army advanced by land and sea. Liu held Taipei and lured the enemy in deep, ambushing them from all sides and annihilating countless enemies. Liu used his 3,000 Black Flag soldiers to fight north and south of Taiwan, fighting bitterly for three months. When the ammunition and rations were exhausted, he raised the white flag and surrendered. The Japanese army believed it to be true and sent marines to land and take over. With a thunderous sound, the landmine exploded, killing and wounding hundreds of Japanese soldiers. Liu had already disguised himself and fled far away on a British ship.

Record of the Remaining Style of Sleeping on Brushwood and Tasting Gall

— Baoqinxuan Master

Our Yue is the place where King Goujian of Yue slept on brushwood and tasted gall. Modern revolutionary martyrs, such as Qiu Jin, Xu Xilin, and Tao Chengzhang, were all born there. The remaining legacy and style have lasted for thousands of years. Recently, the violent Japanese have been rampant, and the whole country is gnashing its teeth. The sound of resisting Japan and saving the country is boiling throughout the country. And in Yuezhong, there are old widows, shepherds, scholars, and gamblers who are generous and enthusiastic to avenge the country's hatred. It is impossible not to record this. The Record of the Remaining Style of Sleeping on Brushwood and Tasting Gall is made.

Bu Shi Among Women Thirty miles away from the city, there is a village called Zhu Chu. Most of the villagers are surnamed Chen. There is an old widow, Madam Shan, who is over sixty years old. She has no son. A daughter is married to the Fu family in the neighboring village. Her husband was in Japan, engaged in the silk business, and the family was quite well-off. Her husband has been dead for more than ten years. Madam Shan owns an inheritance of 20,000 yuan, so she does not have to worry about freezing and starvation. One day, an anti-Japanese propaganda team came to the village to give a speech. Madam Shan also listened to the speech in the crowd. When she heard about the atrocities of the Japanese army and the tragic situation of our soldiers and civilians, she could not help but burst into tears. She said to the people in the team, "The foreign soldiers are so rampant. Is there no loyal minister in China to defend the country? I am old and have no children. If China goes to war with Japan, I am willing to donate half of my property to help the military expenses." Madam Shan had also read books and recognized characters, and old novels such as Yue Zhuan and Three Kingdoms were her only pastime. The old woman has this insight. Why is she so much more than Bu Shi of the Han Dynasty?

Eradicating Stains A shepherd boy, A Si, is from Dongpu. He lost his parents when he was young and lived with his uncle. His uncle ordered A Si to herd sheep. There is an ancient temple where A Si herds sheep. A huge Ajinomoto advertisement is painted on the wall. When A Si was herding sheep, he scraped the wall with a small knife. Three days later, the advertisement below had been scraped off. Only the upper part was short and could not reach. A Si then brought a bamboo ladder to continue scraping the wall. It happened to be seen by the temple owner, who blamed him for destroying the temple wall. A Si argued eloquently, saying that this was an advertisement for Japanese goods. How could it be allowed to exist? Now that I have scraped it off, I have actually eradicated the stains for your temple. You don't appreciate me, but blame me? The temple owner was speechless and had no choice.

Special Storytelling Feng from Shangjia Village is a former Qing Dynasty scholar who failed to pass the imperial examination. He sets up a private school to teach students. His appearance is extremely pedantic. Although Feng is a dullard, he pays close attention to current affairs. After class, he often goes to the village newspaper to read the newspaper. Since the Mukden Incident, Feng's reading of the newspaper has become even more energetic. Feng must go to a small teahouse to drink tea every night. Usually, he just chats casually, but recently he specializes in talking about the atrocities of the Japanese. He extracts materials from the newspaper, adds and subtracts them himself, and imitates storytelling. His oral narration and gestures are vivid and detailed. Most of the listeners are moved. Recently, the business of small teahouses has become prosperous because of this. The villagers all come to listen to this special storytelling.

Sharpening With Care Lai Sanbao, who lives in the same village as Feng, lives by gambling. He is honest, has great strength, and raises his fist at any disagreement. Therefore, people are afraid of him. After hearing Feng's narration of the Japanese atrocities, Sanbao could not help but feel resentful. He specially ordered a pure steel dagger from a blacksmith and played with it day and night. Whenever he wins a gamble, no matter how much or how little, he must withdraw half of it and store it in a small grocery store set up by his wife's uncle. When asked about the meaning of buying a knife and saving money, Sanbao said resolutely, "The dagger is for the evil thieves like Honjo Shigeru, Doihara Kenji, and Yoshizawa. The money is saved to prepare for the travel expenses to the Northeast." Some people ridiculed him for being癡者, but Sanbao never moved. Sharpening with care, vowing to make a quick strike.

Good Horse

— Zui Chi Sheng

For more than ten years, our country has been rising and falling, and has been in civil war. The so-called barbarian struggle and fratricide are not glorious in victory. It is painful to speak of. Only this time, General Ma Zhanshan of Heilongjiang Province was able to resist the violent Japanese with an isolated army. He has fought hard for days and frustrated their fierce attack. Such a record is worthy of admiration by the Chinese people. Looking at his anti-Japanese telegram, his generous words arouse a sense of loyalty and courage in people. With this brave general to support the precarious situation in the dying Northeast, it is enough to make the Japanese bandits look at him with fear. Therefore, the people should express their respect to this General Ma. Everyone said in unison and drank with joy, "Good Horse!"

Presented to General Ma Zhanshan

— Wu Jiu

Two hundred thousand people disarmed together, but the general alone wielded the Lu Yang spear. The Zhang family's pigs and dogs should be ashamed to die. They can recognize the Ma Fubo of Longjiang.

Reminiscing General Ma Zhanshan

— Shi Chuqing

I am sad to see the battle clouds spreading over the Northeast, and the first battle shattered the enemy's courage. Qi said that the general had many ancient meanings, but only because iron and stone are loyal livers.

Swear to express the national crisis and make a miracle. The middle pillar of the rapids is admired by the crowd. The sound of the bugle is silent and the mountain is dark, with 100,000 soldiers and one general.

Three Voices on Guofu Road

— Zhang Yan

Sadness There is A'er from Gaoyou, a Jiangbei native who is not good at it. His personal life is to pull a rickshaw. A'er's wife is not spoiled and loves to eat and drink. Therefore, she is unwilling to let her husband suffer alone. Therefore, every day in the sweltering heat, when we are in the midst of fragrant dreams, before the morning light comes out, we are often awakened by A'er's wife's high-pitched voice selling 洋糖 hot zongzi. Because her voice is clear and sad, like an ape crying in an empty valley, a widow weeping at night, we can't bear to hear it, but there is no way to avoid it. Because it is morning, so-called energetic, there is not much pain. Recently, A'er's wife changed to selling sunflower seeds in the afternoon because the season is winter and the zongzi automatically fell. Because it is evening, it feels even more sad to hear it.

Selling newspapers Since the capital was attacked by the violent Japanese and took the risk of being unrighteous, the sales of the two major newspapers, Shen and Xin, in Shanghai have increased sharply. If you buy these two major newspapers from newspaper vendors after 6:00 or 7:00 PM every night, they will often shake their heads and have no way to respond. It can be seen that when disaster strikes, there are indeed many people who care about national affairs. On Guofu Road, after the fish began to leap, we often heard the voices of many children selling various evening newspapers, high into the clouds. This sang and the other harmonized, which was quite lively.

The sound of cars and horses Although there are many cars and horses in the capital, even Shanghai is not as good. The most complex place for the sound of cars is Guofu Road. Guofu Road is on the left. There is a small train station. The train comes and goes dozens of times a day. It opens in the faint morning light and rests until late at night. Behind Guofu Road is the Executive Yuan, as well as agencies such as civil servants, military参军, and the main计处, and the General Staff. To the right of Guofu is the passage to Central University, the Ministry of Education, the Examination院, and Kongdao, which leads to Xiaguan. Therefore, from early morning to late night every day, we often hear the呜呜 sound of cars, the 轔轔 sound of horse-drawn carriages, the sound of得得 horseshoes, the ding-ding sound of rickshaw bells, and the sound of the small train releasing steam. The sounds respond to each other and there is not a moment of silence. This is a true place where the four directions converge and cars and horses are mixed.

A Record of Mr. Yan's Gourd Divination

— Yan

The gourd divination of the novelist, Mr. Yan Fusun, is remarkably insightful and widely known. All who come to inquire about characters and stop their carriages praise its miraculous nature. The characters he determines emerge from a "sealed gourd," demonstrating ingenious thought and natural inspiration. He keeps a complete set of dictionaries on his desk, and can arbitrarily select two characters to make on-the-spot judgments with incredible speed. Mr. Yan has long been afflicted with illness, and has moved his residence to Lixian Lane on the south side of the Great Horse Road in the French Concession, west of the waterworks. However, he is beset by poverty and illness, and can only勉力 (exhaust his efforts) grind his inkstone, rack his brains, and pour out his heart. His livelihood is very difficult. Gourd divination can be used to predict anything. He now works full-time. My relatives and friends recently consulted him on several matters, and his predictions were strikingly accurate. I will select and record one or two examples to provide material for conversation.

My friend Mr. Liu planned to go to Tianjin. Before his departure, he divined the characters "厄" (è, misfortune) and "少" (shǎo, few). Mr. Yan immediately judged, "The character '厄' reveals a '角' (jiǎo, horn), which must signify '危' (wēi, danger). The character '少' forms '步' (bù, step) because of '止' (zhǐ, stop). Danger is lurking there, so it is better to stop." Mr. Liu hesitated upon hearing this, and then canceled his trip. It was later learned that the day he was scheduled to arrive in Tianjin was precisely when a riot broke out. The gourd divination can indeed be called miraculous.

In the match between the Donghua Football Team and the Norsenburg team, during the first half, Mr. Yan used the characters "甬" (yǒng, brave) and "卡" (kǎ, card) to predict that both sides would be brave but lack strength, and that neither side would prevail. As a result, both teams scored zero, resulting in a tie. Before the final match, a group of fans recommended that Mr. Da Wu go to divine. From the "sealed gourd," he shook out the characters "金" (jīn, gold) and "月" (yuè, moon). Mr. Yan said, "Gold first, moon after. '金' represents the image of breaking a '釜' (fǔ, pot, i.e. '破釜沉舟' pòfǔchénzhōu 'burn one's boats'). Adding '券' (quàn, ticket) to the left side of '月' forms '勝' (shèng, victory). Therefore, if you are determined to win, victory will be assured." In the fierce battle, our team succeeded. Tens of thousands of fans were delighted. The iron pen of Mr. Junping complements our iron army, which is also a good story.

Mr. Huang, an accountant at the Maoxin Shoe Factory, was addicted to dog racing and refused to change his ways. He once shook out the characters "昔" (xī, past) and "狺" (yín, barking) from the gourd. Mr. Yan judged, "First, the character '昔' already has no '手' (shǒu, hand) to '措' (cuò, arrange, i.e., '束手無策' shùshǒuwúcè 'at one's wits end'). Finally, the character '狺' ultimately fears that '犬' (quǎn, dog) will lead to '獄' (yù, prison)." Mr. Huang did not believe this and continued his immersion as before. A few weeks ago, he was indeed imprisoned for embezzling public funds due to losses from dog racing. The predictions were all confirmed. Peng Yongsheng, a partner at Pengfuji Eyeglasses in Sanpailou, along with his fellow villager Hu Zhilin, consulted about their fortunes this spring, shaking out the characters "儉" (jiǎn, frugal) and "佳" (jiā, good). Mr. Yan said, "Looking closely at the character '儉', '人' (rén, person) is in a '險' (xiǎn, dangerous) situation. The character '佳' has a good appearance, but upon further study, it is the top of the character '焦' (jiāo, scorched). If you do not leave quickly this year, you may suffer a '焦頭' (jiāotóu, scorched head) and be in a terrible state." At the time, Mr. Yan made a straightforward judgment based on reason. Unexpectedly, a fire broke out at Pengfuji Eyeglasses a few days ago, and Peng Yongsheng tragically perished in it. Most strangely, it confirmed the "scorched head" prophecy. This matter was spread by a person named Hu. Is Mr. Yan's gourd indeed magical?

Leisurely Chat at the Di Xiang Studio

— Gan Yi

Wang Hu

In this world, people inevitably face both praise and criticism, and both arise from others. It depends on the speaker's perspective. Those who praise Wang Hu say he is thrifty in his personal life, honest as an official, and diligent in his work. Those who criticize Wang Hu say he is fishing for fame and reputation, deceiving the world and stealing a name. Should we believe the praisers or the critics? Perhaps the criticisms are warranted? But right and wrong will always be publicly judged. Hu's courtesy name is Tieshan. He is from Zhili, entered the Hanlin Academy, and was assigned to be a county magistrate after completing his studies. He served in Junlian, Sichuan, where he was praised as a "Wen Weng" (a wise and benevolent official). At that time, Cen Yunjie (Chunxuan) was the governor of Guangxi and heard of Hu's virtue. He requested Hu be transferred to Guangxi to command the unified army. When Cen Yunjie was promoted to governor of Guangdong, he recommended Hu to be the garrison commander of Qinlian. Many bandits had long plagued the counties of Qinlian. Hu led his troops to fight the bandits, but they were defeated and the city fell. Hu was stripped of his position and investigated. After a long time, the governor of the east, Xi Qingbi (Liang), requested that his original position be restored. He was appointed to the Southeast Road of Jilin. He was selfless in discussing politics and diligent in handling affairs. After the establishment of the Republic of China, he successively served as a magistrate in Zhili and was promoted to governor of the capital. He was transferred to the Hunan Provincial High Commissioner, but did not take office. He was appointed as a censor in the Board of Audit. He was known as the "Iron-Faced Censor." Qi Yaoshan had long managed civil affairs in Jiangsu and sought to leave. The governor of Jiangsu, Li Chun, recommended several people to the government, with Hu at the top of the list. The government removed Qi Yaoshan from his position and ordered Hu to succeed him. Hu lingered in the northern capital and did not go. One day, the whole city spread the news that the new provincial governor had arrived and had taken up residence in the official residence, awaiting the day to take office. Everyone was greatly surprised. Hu had taken the Jinpu train, crossed the river in disguise, and walked alone to the small train station (the trains that connect the inner and outer city of Nanjing are called small trains). He boarded the train and entered the city, then walked alone to the provincial governor's office. The guards stopped him and asked, "Who are you here to see?" Hu smiled without answering, but said, "I am qualified to enter." The guards did not dare to make a decision on their own and asked their superior. The superior was from the north and, seeing Hu's face, recognized him. He knew that Hu usually liked to disguise himself as figures like Shi Gong (a legendary upright official). He bowed respectfully and said, "Are you perhaps the new provincial governor?" Hu said, "Yes." The superior said, "We have been waiting for a long time," and escorted him in. Several followers also arrived from other routes. The news spread, and those who sought to pay their respects filled the door. After Hu took office, a candidate circuit intendant came to pay his respects. Hu ordered the middle gate to be opened and personally greeted him at the foot of the steps. With a solemn expression, he said, "Commissioner, how have you been since we last met?" The man stammered and could not answer. After sitting for a short time, Hu ordered the guest to be seen off. The man remained uneasy and speechless. He visited three times, and Hu treated him the same way each time. When Hu was serving in Sichuan, the man, as a circuit intendant, served as the bandit suppression commissioner and had criticized Hu to the governor. Hu, because of his lower rank, did not dare to resist. Now, he had begun to retaliate in a humorous way. Therefore, the man was not employed during Hu's tenure and left for another place. His actions were like this. Some say that Hu rose from a county magistrate to a high-ranking official, able to put into practice the saying "Civil officials should not be greedy for money," and his character is naturally higher than others. But his heart is small and easily filled with pride, and his hypocrisy and eagerness for praise cannot be concealed.

Speaking Club

A Country Bumpkin Arrives in Shanghai Again (21)

— Bao Tianxiao

"Meat" is the most fashionable thing in Shanghai recently. No matter what film is shown in the cinema, the advertisements always use large woodcuts with the words "sensual" and "meaty." No matter where a novel is published, it is about "meat," "spirit," and being intoxicated by the description of meat. There are even so-called "salty meat shops," which are more convenient than brothels. Transactions are made on the spot, and goods are sold in stock. Everyone in Shanghai, whether they are from Shanghai or not, has become Chen Ping of the Han Dynasty, and everyone is going to cut a piece of it.

Because meat is enough to move people, the color of meat has also become fashionable. The country bumpkin thinks: "I must have seen it wrong." At first, I saw several girls wearing very beautiful clothes, but I wondered why they didn't wear socks. I thought it was because it was summer. Now I understand. Then, I just saw several shop assistants in the shops here who were shirtless. Maybe they have never been shirtless, but everyone is wearing a flesh-colored undershirt.

That girl still grabbed the country bumpkin and wouldn't let go.

"Let go, we can talk nicely." The country bumpkin was surrounded. He felt a little embarrassed to be grabbed by a woman on the street.

"Our business has been bad these past two days, so we are burning incense to the road to improve our luck. Why did you come to stamp it out? You are bringing us bad luck."

"Burning incense to the road? Why don't you burn it at home? Instead, you burn it along the street."

"Burning it at home or burning it along the road is none of your business. You shouldn't have come to bring us bad luck." That girl grabbed the country bumpkin and wouldn't let him go.

Fortunately, a passerby knew that the country bumpkin was surrounded and rushed to mediate. He said, "He meant well, he was afraid that you would burn your clothes. Who knew what you were burning incense to the road for? Stamping out the fire is no big deal, you can just get some more scraps of paper to burn."

With a few words, he finally helped the country bumpkin out of the siege. The country bumpkin quickly thanked this friend who helped him out of the siege, and said while panting:

"What do these women do? They are so fierce! Their strength is even greater than ours men. Once they grab you, you can't shake them off."

"These are all prostitutes. They gather in this area. Even if you don't provoke them, they will still pull and tug at you. What's more, you went to talk to them. They see that you are not like the old Shanghai people, and they just said that you stamped out the fire they were burning to the road, using this as an excuse to rip you off."

The country bumpkin had heard people say that there were many prostitutes in Shanghai. But I didn't expect them to be so fierce, surrounding me like this. How can the Shanghai authorities allow them to pull people like that along the road without prohibiting them? In our village, there are definitely no such shameless women.

Gold Prices Continue to Climb Relentlessly

Continuing to Rise Beyond Twenty-Four Taels

All Day in the Midst of Furious Winds and Rain. Yesterday's gold market saw significant changes, with morning highs and afternoon lows, followed by a recovery in the later market. Throughout the day, there were fluctuations of twenty taels, the situation was chaotic, with no real confidence, and people were confused. As a result, there was a sharp increase of more than twenty-four taels. Financial departments in businesses were constantly changing, and the silver market moved in a different direction, with the pound rising and the dollar falling, which had been expected the day before. Only the European market was relatively good, with gold prices opening high and immediately breaking through the 660-tael mark. There was a rush of large-scale purchases, and many were covering their short positions. In addition, both official and unofficial exchange rates were tight, with exchange rates narrowing by three notches. The market felt particularly strong, already breaking through the 70-tael mark. Unexpectedly, speculators and large syndicates seized the opportunity to dump their holdings, and also because foreign exchange suddenly became easier to obtain, and banks were willing to sell. There were also reports from abroad that European and American countries were planning to maintain silver prices. In reality, cash reserves had increased compared to before, but there was no buying power. Because of this, they retreated quickly, falling more than twenty taels sharply. The market was expected to be weak in the later market because there is no market on Wednesdays as is typical for the foreign exchange market. But because Indian exchange rates fell repeatedly, buying interest in the market was strong, again exceeding the 60-tael mark, with a surge of more than ten taels. It is predicted that the major players expect a decline this morning.

Early Morning Fluctuations were Extremely Frightening. From the early opening, the price rose by eighteen taels and eight qian (0.88 taels), to 662.5 taels. Major players were indeed up eight-sevenths of a fen, and forward prices up thirteen-sixteenths of a fen. The price decreased from 66 taels and 3 qian to 59 taels and 5 qian. In a moment, Yifeng Yong, Dadecheng, Yuanxing Yong, Yifeng, and foreign merchants such as Qiaozhifu (乔直夫) competed to buy. Cotton Market Enters Another Slump

The cotton market has turned weak due to the sluggishness of American cotton. The gold market remains strong, but bullish investors are cashing out their positions as the market rises. In reality, spot cotton trading is stagnant, and factories have no intention of purchasing local cotton due to the high prices, which are being undercut by foreign cotton. As a result, the cotton market is softening again. There was some anticipation of a short squeeze earlier this month, but now spot cotton trading has halted, and the tight money market has led to the unloading of purchased cotton. Consequently, the market has loosened and is trending downward.

Recent Speculative Buying Emerges. The Shanghai cotton futures market opened with a slightly bullish sentiment due to steady American cotton prices and rising gold prices, with all months rising by two mace. The market turned weak during the second and third sessions, ultimately falling by 1.5 mace. In the afternoon, near-month bullish investors emerged, further loosening the market, with all months falling by 1.5 to 2 mace. The total volume traded for the day was 74,300 bales. Rongxing traded 1,900 bales, Gengfeng 5,100 bales, Yiyu 3,200 bales, and Dafeng 1,900 bales. Buyers included Changfeng with 2,300 bales, Yifeng with 2,700 bales, and Shenchang with 2,300 bales. Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning, the market for all months generally showed a trend of initially bullishness followed by flatness. Initially, the prices of imported wheat for near- and far-term delivery generally rose by 0.02 to 0.03 yuan. However, in the afternoon sessions, the flour market was not good, and the selling of imported wheat futures continued. Factories would purchase as soon as prices were favorable. Practically speaking, it was difficult to be overly bullish, as both local and out-of-town traders could not bear the pressure of dumping after ordering imported wheat. As a result, this month was unchanged, December was down by 0.01 yuan, January was unchanged, February was down by 0.02 yuan, March was up by 0.01 yuan, and April was unchanged.

Silk and Tea: Pingshui Pearl Tea Sales to Europe Slightly Active

Yesterday, in the tea market of foreign firms in Shanghai, there was slightly more interest from European and American merchants in Huzhou Pingshui green tea. Among them, the top two or three grades of pearl tea saw relatively active trading, and market prices were quite firm. The market for Tunxi Zhenmei and Zhenmei Needle green tea seemed more active than before, but tea prices were low, and tea merchants were generally pessimistic. Furthermore, the sales of Wuyuan Gaozhuang Zhenmei and Gongxi green tea remained stagnant, and the overall trend was not good.

Coal: Changxing Coal Supply Fails to Meet Demand

Since the Zhejiang provincial government took over the Changxing Coal Mine, daily coal production has increased to more than 300 tons. Most of the power plants and silk factories in Zhejiang province use this coal, so sales are quite large, and the daily supply cannot meet the demand. As a result, very little coal arrives in Shanghai, and prices are firm. The latest prices for various types of coal are as follows: Changxing lump coal, 11.5 taels; Changxing mixed coal, 8.75 taels; Guangxing lump coal, 12.5 taels; Guangxing selected coal, 9.75 taels.

Miscellaneous News

One hundred and sixty bales of Huzhou silk shipped to the United States.

Six hundred barrels of tobacco leaves arrived from the United States.

One thousand bales of American cotton imported yesterday.

More than three hundred bolts of woolens shipped from England.

One thousand seven hundred barrels of wire nails shipped from London.

More than six thousand bales of rayon shipped from Europe.

One thousand two hundred barrels of paint shipped from London.

Three hundred tons of cigarettes shipped to the South Seas Islands.

Six thousand bags of refined sugar shipped to various ports along the Yangtze River.

Youth Corner

Candor

— Xu Shui Lin

A Reply from an Actress

Yin Jun,

I truly didn't expect that you would have such a request of me. Perhaps it's my fault for having led you on. But I'm always like this with friends, no, not friends, acquaintances. I'm always like this with acquaintances, and not only with acquaintances, but with all the audience. It's not surprising that others behave like this toward me. Not to mention a year, there are always several instances within a month, or even a week. It's rare for me to not receive one of these kinds of annoying letters every morning.

The words you use to compliment and praise me, others have used them to death, and there are others who are ten or a hundred times more nauseating than what you've said. At first, I was indeed somewhat moved, but now I'm completely used to it. It only arouses my revulsion. Sometimes, if the writing or wording is good, it amuses me.

Heavy makeup, enchanting looks, this has become a necessity in my daily life. If I don't do this, I can't attract people's attention. If I can't attract people's attention, then my business will fail, and my reputation will fall. Which theater owner would still hire me? How would my life and the lives of my family be sustained? This has already become a habit, and it involves the role of professionalization and commercialization. Seducing people is a sin in ordinary society, but for us, it's an art, a profession. Asking an actress not to seduce people is like telling people not to eat. Is that possible?

In the beginning, this seduction was very awkward and embarrassing. I thought it was a sin, especially offstage. But now I'm used to it. I'm very happy to see so many men chasing after me. I often use many inhumane methods to embarrass them, to trample on them, yet they still follow me with gentle smiles.

Some give up after being tricked once or twice, while others continue to follow me even after being tricked repeatedly. Some, though normally very stingy, become completely different people once they're hooked. If I set my mind to it, they would be willing to go bankrupt. Some fools spend a great price but never get the chance to even once. Some smart ones get the opportunity without spending anything. In the beginning, some people got lucky. But in recent years, no one has gotten a bargain with me anymore. Among the group of people chasing me recently, the only one who can get a bargain with me is you, but you're not one of those kinds of people.

I have an impulse to tease people, but with you, aside from the most ordinary jokes, I can confidently say that I've never teased you once. Because you are sensitive, honest, intelligent, and refined, I am very respectful of you. It certainly exceeds the feelings of so-called acquaintances and reaches the level of friendship. This is certainly why I have harmed you.

I can't bear to hurt you, can't bear to push you further into confusion. It's not that all your true feelings have moved me. Your letter is precisely the opportunity for me to tease you. I now hate that you didn't meet me a few years ago. At that time, my habits weren't so bad yet. But it's impossible now. In my spirit and in my body, it seems I've become diseased. What do you still want from me? Of course, I won't just casually go with you. No, if you were to be insistent to the point of seeking death, I could definitely be with you. But what the outcome will be, it's absolutely impossible to predict. After much thought, it seems it's better to separate. I know that you will feel pain, and I will also feel a lot of sadness over time. But it's still better to separate.

Your estimations of my thoughts, if it were a few years ago, would have been very accurate. Although some of them don't match the facts, most are correct. Perhaps they are also correct for the average young woman. But not now, not for me. An objective estimation to completely coincide with the feelings of the person involved, I think it's practically impossible. I might as well tell you what I subjectively feel, and you must keep this a secret from the world. I trust your integrity and believe you wouldn't use this to retaliate against me or blackmail me.

A strong body like yours is what I need. A sensitive feeling like yours is what I desire. But a material environment like yours is what I can't be satisfied with.

What I seek now is material enjoyment. In other words, cars, mansions, pianos, phonographs, wireless telephones, wine, meat, bright lights, vibrant colors.

Sharp sounds, the servitude of humans and animals, and everything that can be bought with money to stimulate my nerves.

Lofty ideals cannot blind my consciousness. The flames of material things warm my soul. If you could provide me with that kind of woman, I would still have to act. If I still have to act, then those people needed for business, such as drama critics, authoritative journalists, and wealthy and influential long-term patrons, will still have to be socialized with. Given that I socialize as usual, can my nominal status as a married woman scare away their ambition to pursue me? Having become accustomed to romance, can I suddenly put on a straight face to everyone and reject requests beyond friendship? Even if my name is your wife, if my behavior doesn't improve, can you endure this kind of insult?

If my current savings have already reached the limit I've set, I would give up my career. If such a person wants me, I would go with you and not be afraid of your poverty. But my savings are only enough for one or two years of living. Can't I rest for a year or two and then go back to the sea? At that time, I'll have to say, "Why did I do this in the first place?"

My relationship with you also stems from business, from being a customer to being an acquaintance to being a friend. After we became acquainted, your clever mind has helped me a lot with the matching of outfits, the depth of expressions, the harmonization of music, and the arrangement of sentences. In other words, you have helped me a lot in business. To put it more elegantly, you have helped me a lot in art. If I left the stage life after going with you, most of your advantages in my eyes would be completely lost. You definitely wouldn't be able to excite me as you do now. At that time, I wouldn't be sure whether I would change my heart toward you.

Although I don't want a husband like you, I do want a lover like you. When I first met you, I thought you came with the same purpose as them. Later, I saw that you didn't. I thought you really loved art. Who knew you had an even bigger ambition: to completely seize me. This is truly something I didn't expect.

Do you remember the dozens of times we parted after a show? I told you to send me back. Several times you brought me to my door, but I pretended not to let you in. There were also several times you brought me inside my house but didn't let you into my room, didn't let you sit on my bed. All these were just to arouse your further requests. Who knew you would listen like a child, telling you what to do and doing it. At that time, I both loved you and respected you, but I also hated you: loved your intelligence, respected your honesty, hated your lack of understanding. Now I know that you didn't lack understanding, but rather that you saw the meaning in a deeper layer.

Now I'm clearly expressing to you that I can't be

your wife, I can only be your lover. If you are willing to be my lover, I am willing to provide everything I have to make you happy. Whether you want a month, a year, two years, however long you want to, whenever. Even if I leave this place, no matter where I go, as long as there is a chance to meet, you will always have the right to have me.

The difference between a lover and a couple is that they each are not responsible for the other person's behavior and personality. A sincere person like you, and all your life's ideals, are not suitable for an irregular woman like me. A romantic person like me, for business reasons, shouldn't have a solemn husband like you. If we are lovers, I believe we will always get along.

You might say, "Since you know that your behavior is irregular, won't you ever change it?"

Yes, I don't plan to change my behavior in the near future, because I don't have the concept of family prestige, and I don't have the responsibility to consider the reputation of my parents and brothers. And society isn't worth criticizing our behavior. It's even more unnecessary to talk about not being able to marry in the future because of irregular behavior. If I want to marry, there are many men who are waiting for me to choose. The reason I am like this is of course due to business, but I also enjoy it a little. According to my estimation, there are indeed some adult women who envy our kind of life, but they are suppressed by various social constraints and cannot realize their desires. Even if society hinders them a lot and supervises them strictly, in this bustling city, not only in the lower class, but even in families claiming to be upper class, how many women stay true to one man? I really don't believe it, but it's just that they have heavy doors and deep courtyards, and outsiders can't know.

This is my shortcoming, and it's the reason why I refuse to be your nominal wife. If you are willing to be my lover, you can stay with me for a long time, which is equivalent to being my actual husband. When you don't want to anymore, you can leave me at any time. How free and worthwhile is that? There's no harm to you in terms of economics and reputation, but it's beneficial to me.

I'm 25 years old now, and I'll do this business for at most ten more years. If you were to say that you could first be my lover for ten years, and after ten years, when I leave the stage life, we could officially marry, no, not ten years, as soon as I've met my savings limit, I'll leave the stage life. If you can condescend and be my lover, I believe I can work even harder to complete my plan in the shortest possible time. As soon as I nominally become your wife, I will immediately correct my behavior and be willing to be bound and supervised by you.

Otherwise, you wait for me for ten years. You're only 23 years old this year, and getting married at 33 isn't too late. During these ten years, I'll also subsidize you with a considerable amount of money, which is stronger than what you'd spend living with me. You can also get sexual satisfaction in casual relationships.

You might scold me for being shameless, but I'm not ashamed. I'm telling you my thoughts very honestly and sincerely. I know my weaknesses myself. I'm like a wild horse now, and I can't bear to be tied down anymore. If I intended to deceive you, I would agree to what you said in your letter now. After you've fallen into my trap, I won't worry about you not following me in the future due to the pressure of life. Although you are very sensitive, you lack experience. I believe you won't be able to see through my flaws for a while. By that time, I will definitely have a way to make you believe me without a doubt. Even if you get a slight whiff of something, you'll have to temporarily endure it because of your own reputation and face. Perhaps you'll even help me hide it. But I'm not willing to do that. I can't bear to harm a good soul, and my own scheming is too tiring.

Otherwise, you have spent a lot of energy on me recently, and there should be some price. I'm willing to give you back a sum of money that's enough for you to maneuver with. You have many life plans, and you can use this money to spend. If you have a very good result in the near future and reach the level that I can be satisfied with, I will come to you at any time. At the same time, you should note that if you allow me this plan, I will also work harder in the future. But you may not want my money, thinking that it's unclean.

I am now in a state of contradiction. Since I don't want to be bound by you, I also want to make you my final destination. There isn't a woman in the world who doesn't want her man to be exclusively hers, but I now want to possess many men over time. This is another contradiction.

A man like you, I believe I won't meet again in my life except for you. If I lose you, even though there are many men chasing me now, I won't feel any embarrassment. When I'm old and my looks fade, I'll have to think of you. The older I get, the more I'll think of you. Your sincerity and honesty have indeed moved me.

Given all that, why don't I just fold my sails now and go with you? But how can I give up my unusual position now? Others think I'm a singer who excites millions, so they always think I must have something magical. I also use other people's psychology to use many magical things. In fact, to be honest, I'm as ordinary as the women of the world. I think many of the miracles of historical beauties are mostly passed down by changing times and circumstances, or they were arbitrarily laid out by several or one bored writer to satisfy their ideal pornography.

The many words you use to compliment me, I feel sad inside when I see them. I use this psychology to make others go crazy with their excessive compliments, but I'm not willing to tease you like that. You see me as too magical, which is no different from digging an unclosable chasm between you and me. I've told you many things above that are beyond your expectations and that you don't know. If it came from the mouth of a third party, you would never believe it and would even think it was a malicious insult. I'm telling you now in my own handwriting on paper, and you should believe that I am indeed an ordinary woman like the women of the world. There is no magic at all, and I lack many of the virtues that ordinary women should have. (To be continued)

Social News

Marshal Foch's War Diaries

— Translated by Gu Angruo

Regarding the French-Belgian area, I believe that after the Allied Supreme Commander obtains the consent of the three supreme commanders of the French, British, and American forces and the chief of staff of the Belgian army, he should be an advisor to the Allied governments.

The first and second items of the armistice conditions belong to military necessity, and the third item belongs to the guarantee of reparations. Are these guarantees sufficient to guarantee the reparations required by France and its allied countries, especially Belgium? If so, what will happen to these occupied areas after the reparations are paid? Will our army continue to occupy them, or will it secede from a part of them, or will it establish an independent autonomous country as a neutral buffer zone? Does the armistice completely preserve these issues? The Allied Supreme Commander should study these issues in detail with the governments of the countries concerned in advance. The armistice should give our army sufficient guarantees so that the conditions I put forward during the peace talks can force the enemy to submit.

For this reason, I should always have close contact with important personnel of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs should also often notify me of its opinions and the armistice conditions of the Allied governments. In this way, I can determine that the military guarantees and the diplomatic guarantees will not neglect one another, and I can also fulfill my responsibilities to France and the Allied governments.

I asked Mr. Clemenceau in a letter, if he agrees with this idea, please notify me of who from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to contact.

I believe that the most important thing is to study the political conditions of the armistice in detail in advance to prevent future changes. The armistice is related to the cessation of large armies, and the main conditions of the peace treaty should be included in the armistice articles. What will the future changes be, so that we can avoid unexpected blows?

Prime Minister Clemenceau wanted to maintain the government's free action, so he refused to appoint important officials from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to contact me in his reply letter on October 23.

In fact, the armistice conditions must be decided by the Allied governments, and the drafting of the articles must naturally be handled by the Allied governments.

President Wilson has submitted this issue to the Allied governments, and he has notified the German government to negotiate with the military advisors of the Allied countries. However, whether or not the armistice treaty is concluded, and the details of the conditions, must be completely decided by the Allied governments themselves.

The Allied governments have no reason to oppose President Wilson,

The principle of fourteen points as the basis for peace, but if necessary, a few points can be revised. If the enemy fully accepts the armistice conditions, the Allied governments cannot oppose the ceasefire, (To be continued)

Youth Corner

The Sorrow of an Instructor

— Zhu Hongxi

Because the instructor had just arrived at the school and was not yet very clear about the situation within, he felt somewhat uneasy.

He asked his fellow townsman, Mr. Zhang, with utmost sincerity. He inquired whether students in the past had been interested in military drills, whether students could obey the orders of the military instructor and attend drills on time, and what attitude the principal and faculty held towards military training, etc. As a result, Mr. Zhang's answers were quite satisfactory to the instructor.

The instructor thought, this is a very good thing. Students can obey the orders of the military instructor, and can maintain discipline when attending military drills.

A burst of nameless joy suddenly erupted from within his heart.

School was about to begin, and faculty and students were gradually increasing in number. People were constantly coming and going in the dormitories and dining hall. Experience told him that the school was about to return to its state before the summer vacation. The instructor wore a gray Chinese twill military uniform, a diagonal leather belt across his shoulder, a dark gray military cap on his head, and black leather leggings on his feet. He strode around the school in high spirits, with a sincere and solemn expression on his face.

On the day school started, the instructor had no classes, so he quietly sat alone in his room reading the newspaper. He occasionally thought of his past monotonous life and felt satisfied with his current life. Finally, he could not help but harbor a hope for his future.

However, the instructor was a person trained in conscience. He was extremely opposed to using the guise of a military man to get promoted and make a fortune.

The next afternoon, the instructor began teaching according to the school's scheduled timetable. Before going to the drill ground, he first ordered the school worker to blow the bugle several times. He then moved towards the drill ground, holding the roll book. Arriving at the drill ground, the instructor quickly looked around, but could not see any students coming for drills. He then ordered the school worker to blow the bugle a few more times. When the bugle sounded, the double strikes of the class bell also rang. Only then did he understand that the students had not yet come to the drill ground because it was not yet time for class. After the bell stopped, the instructor saw a few students in short clothes running towards the drill ground. After about five minutes, more than ten people had gathered on the drill ground. The instructor opened the roll book and counted the names. As a result, less than one-fifth of the students had come to drill. This made the instructor somewhat suspicious, and a feeling of displeasure arose in his heart. However, the instructor thought again, school has not been in session for very long. Perhaps the students who did not come to drill were busy with other things and had not had time to arrive. A kind of hope surged up from his heart again. He felt relieved.

The instructor was a person who advocated saving the country with conscience. He was extremely critical of those soldiers who kept wives and concubines but failed to fulfill their duties. Once, he had openly expressed his opinions in front of many students, saying that the most hateful people in the country were those who only knew how to eat but did not know how to work, especially those who ate public funds but did not work for the public. Finally, he said,

He had been ordered by the central government to come to this school as a military instructor. He had to achieve excellent results in the military training of this school to be worthy of the central government and of himself. Otherwise, he would be extremely unwilling to do it. Rather than eating this kind of nominal meal, it would be better not to eat it at all... At that time, none of the students were not moved by the instructor's words.

On Saturday afternoon, the instructor took the roll book to drill again. No, it was to the classroom. After the second bugle stopped, the instructor ran into Classroom No. 9. Walking into the classroom, the instructor felt somewhat doubtful again. Why were there so few people present out of more than a hundred? The instructor was at a loss. But the instructor thought, today is Saturday. Many schools do not have classes on Saturday afternoons. It is really inappropriate for the school to schedule this class on Saturday afternoon. They all did not come to class today, there is a reason for it.

Time passed day by day, and the instructor understood the situation of the school more and more each day. After two weeks, he learned from the facts. His courage, his hope, had gradually disappeared. He had begun to immerse himself in sorrow, disappointment, and negativity.

……………………………………

It has been almost two months since the school started, but the instructor's plans have still not been implemented. The instructor's hopes have still not been realized. The instructor is still as sad and disappointed as before.

Everyone Prepare Yourselves

— Gong Jingzhong

After the territory of our country in the Northeast, such as Shenyang, Yingkou, Changchun, Andong, etc., were occupied by Japanese imperialism due to our lack of preparation, the entire country, from top to bottom, felt a sense of shared hatred and wanted to kill them all as quickly as possible. Therefore, in these dozens of days, our compatriots, regardless of age, have been fighting for the cause of resisting Japan and saving the country. We will never give up until we recover our lost territories. Since this is the case, everyone prepare yourselves. Now I will explain it by category for the reference of my patriotic compatriots.

Soldiers 丨 Prepare fast guns and sharp cannons, heads, hot blood, to go to the battlefield to die.

Workers 丨 Prepare calloused hands and feet to rush to manufacture cannons, airplanes...all military supplies.

Literati 丨 Prepare to rack your brains and shed bloody tears, to write passionate and stirring articles.

Farmers 丨 Prepare hoes and plows, and go with the eastward-bound soldiers to immigrate to the Northeast and cultivate the fields.

Merchants 丨 Prepare to lose some capital, actively improve domestic products, and permanently sever economic ties with Japan.

Students 丨 Prepare to study hard on the one hand and actively practice military drills and charge into battle on the other.

Women 丨 Prepare to be comfort teams, relief teams, rear defense forces, and cooks. In particular, prepare to painstakingly educate children to become great citizens and not forget the great enemy of Japan.

Children 丨 Prepare abundant knowledge, noble cultivation, and healthy bodies to become good citizens in the future, so that China can become prosperous and strong, and avenge your fathers and brothers who died for the country.

Elderly people 丨 Prepare to stay in the rear and raise children.

Those with courage may as well bring out the spirit of "wrapped in horsehide after death," rush to the front with gray hair to kill a few Japanese, so that the enemy is a little timid and knows that the hearts of the Chinese people have not completely died.

Compatriots in the rear 丨 Prepare to starve, gnaw on grass and tree roots, and transport millet to the front lines, so that the soldiers are full and strong and can kill the enemy well.

Overseas Chinese 丨 Prepare to raise a large amount of funds and send them back to serve the motherland.
